####  孤舟垂钓  
##### 11238#       发表于 2015-7-24 01:51




三日月两个版本当然不一样了，香织版整个伴奏都比丽奈版的安静，一方面是风格上凸显香织的柔和性格，另一方面是如果伴奏太强solo就听不到了，缺乏转折的能力所以没有高扬感<img src="https://static.saraba1st.com/image/smiley/face/30.gif" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"> 丽奈版因为solo实力强所以整个演奏过程几个章节起伏转折的感觉都展现的很好。有些地方我甚至听出来星球大战的感觉，浩瀚星空中日月齐舞的景象，鸟肌。

不过有给日亚发邮件问过，日亚报数是按过POS机的数量报的，凡是日亚销售的商品全部要过POS机

所以不用纠结了，该怎么买还怎么买

O榜本身也是根据取样店推算的数据，不可能完全覆盖整个市场的







-----

####  alerbe  
##### 11389#       发表于 2015-7-29 19:39



 本帖最后由 alerbe 于 2015-7-29 19:43 编辑 

第三卷最不合理的地方就是BG线的发展。前一章小黄就用“我们毕竟只是朋友”差点把秀一线直接捅死了，到了最后一章莫名奇妙的送个生日礼物就成了。 另外就是小黄嘴炮明日香这段，我之前读的时候感觉完全不如剧透的那么有力，明日香的反驳是很软弱的。这些问题上，动画改编还是大有可为的，站前演奏会和学园祭都应该实打实的做出来，这些都是加分的地方。

####  孤舟垂钓  
##### 11392#       发表于 2015-7-30 00:18




要出2期最好连续出，有机会像白箱那样展现后劲，毕竟故事性越来越强，1期13集里有7集都在铺垫，第13集也仅仅给人戛然而止的感觉，“这就结束了？”这样的疑问。考虑到课题曲的时效性，也是今年做最好。拖得太久，作品好不容易积累起的人气就会散掉大半了。不过参照Clannad档期，果然最早还是要明年1月才有可能2期吧。

####  孤舟垂钓  
##### 11431#       发表于 2015-8-1 23:12




双簧管这位其实蛮有意思的，如果有刻意关注的话，你会发现她经常出现在画面黄金分割点上(无论是左侧还是右侧），也就是说即便是群像背景，也是那种很容易让人注意到的位置，无声的强调“注意：这个人很重要，所以我反复让她出现”，更不用提特写镜头。

####  alerbe  
##### 11457#       发表于 2015-8-3 19:50



 本帖最后由 alerbe 于 2015-8-3 19:58 编辑 

京都府今年比赛的初中组结果
[http://www.kyoto-suiren.jp/brasscon/2015/ca.htm](http://www.kyoto-suiren.jp/brasscon/2015/ca.htm)


74个参赛学校，22个金赏，3个晋级名额，真是惨烈。  4号的普罗旺斯之后11个学校选，大部分课题曲都选的2号春之道，这个也比较简单一些。

明天开始高中组。 5日还有一组。不过最有意思的是明天下午那拨，看日程表，洛南，橘，东宇冶几乎就是挨着出场的，算是个巧合吧。

<blockquote><a href="httphttps://bbs.saraba1st.com/2b/forum.php?mod=redirect&amp;goto=findpost&amp;pid=29746954&amp;ptid=1085129" target="_blank">tenjou 发表于 2015-8-3 19:59</a>

74个参赛学校。。。这么看来駄目金已经很厉害了，尤其是顺位高的那些。


----发送自 STAGE1 App for Andro ...</blockquote>
初中组是非常激烈的，日本全国3000所学校参赛，高中组的话差不多有1800所学校，机会多一点，但是难度也更高了，因为强校掌握的资源更多。另外北宇冶中学今年是个银。


刚才在2ch看有些人回忆，初中有些强校是每天练4个小时吹奏加2个小时队列的。

####  结标淡希  
##### 11487#       发表于 2015-8-5 23:33




石原：最麻烦的是发现错误的时候。“啊，这里搞错了！”——每当发觉时真是让人……虽然实际并不是由我来修正，但对工作人员说“这里请修正一下”时真的很累。

山田：作品最早发表时，久美子光脚坐在椅子上的宣传图（下图），那是负责角色设计的池田晶子与石原和我拼命摆pose拍照片，最后在自叹“完美！”中制作完成的，然而……悠风号的中央，排水管上有一个圆环，看上去显然是个把手指伸进去的环。小号等乐器会将手指勾进那个环里，于是心想悠风号也一样，想当然地把手指伸了进去，得意洋洋地上交了成品。结果乐器作监高桥博行非常难以启齿地说道“咦，那不是伸手指的地方，也许是用来排水的……”（笑），当然之后立刻修正了。



高桥太辛苦了.....那么这个pose的原型到底是谁（



动画企划阶段，原作只出了第一卷，我们以为就那样完结了....所以你们根本没有想到会是BG结局吧(<img src="https://static.saraba1st.com/image/smiley/face/161.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

####  maertz  
##### 11488#       发表于 2015-8-5 23:34




这个访谈好有趣<img src="https://static.saraba1st.com/image/smiley/face/07.gif" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">


——本作角色众多，除了细心描写以外还有其他的考虑吗？


石原：首先要设计全体成员的角色，这一点相当辛苦。他们不是路人，虽然有的人物没有直接登场，但每个成员都有名字。尽管不是很详细，但在设计角色时会加入“这个孩子是这种类型”这样的设定。如此一来，他们就会像程序般自己运行。然后演出会根据这些设定让他们动起来。“这两个人的关系不好”“这两个人正在交往”，诸如这样的设定。所以后面的集数中明确的关系，在不知不觉中做过铺垫。


“正在交往”<img src="https://static.saraba1st.com/image/smiley/face/91.gif" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">大号夫妇还有钻头夫妇吗



另外给小说画封面的绘师也很喜欢优子，经常看到在推上画夏优

####  dxxtiger

 本帖最后由 dxxtiger 于 2015-8-6 02:21 编辑 
<blockquote>山田：说到第八集，就是浓烈的爱情戏（笑）。

石原：叶月失恋那段也很棒。

山田：叶月坠入爱河的那段也很可爱。我们想要好好守护原作中叶月的人物形象，不想让她显得太可怜。另外，久美子对丽奈是一直线，所以她没有预想到叶月的失恋。他们各自的箭头指向不同，这一点很有趣。</blockquote>
这段真是喷了
 <blockquote>石原：但那还是因为原作就有充分的描写。比如晴香作为部长所处的微妙立场，真的描写得很出色。动画企划阶段，原作只出了第一卷，我们以为就那样完结了。后来听说要出第二卷，拿到了原作的情节。比如说有一个名叫铠冢霙的吹双簧管的二年级女生，对她的描写遵照了第二卷中出现的设定。此外还有明日香的身世。最终回取得进军关西大赛的资格时，明日香的表情看上去并不怎么高兴，关于这一点读过原作第二、第三卷就会明白。动画至此完结，其实那里可以做出改动，但既然存在原作的二、三卷，我觉得还是不改为好，于是就让明日香露出了那样的表情。</blockquote>

居然真的是在只读完第一卷，拿到后面剧情纲要的情况下开始企划的

####  孤舟垂钓  
##### 11491#       发表于 2015-8-6 07:15



<blockquote>山田：原作中这里演奏的曲子是校歌，动画改成了《暴れん坊将軍》。

石原：观众和我们都没有听过北宇治高中的校歌，因而难以判断演奏的好坏。所以这里选了一首耳熟能详、朗朗上口的曲子。

山田：另外第一集我在“樱花”上竭尽了全力。

石原：我的话……仔细看可以发现六地藏站那里有燕子在飞。</blockquote>

-----

####  孤舟垂钓  
##### 11492#       发表于 2015-8-6 07:20



<blockquote>石原：第四集是社团的氛围变得积极向上的故事，观看时心情很好。令人印象深刻的是泷老师所说的“觉得不可能吗？我觉得能办到”，虽然陈腐但我很喜欢这句话。

山田：我非常重视泷老师在说“你们”和“我们”时的区别。两者都会出现，这两个词代表着泷老师两种不同的立场。</blockquote>
确实“你们”“我们”是很重要的体现团队和谐程度的指标。 <blockquote>石原：“想吹得更好”——久美子一边叫喊，一边在宇治桥上奔跑的场景。虽然实际上并不是叫喊而是独白，但那段场面真的非常出色。

山田：这部作品中有许多意识到肺活量的演出。在最棒的场景中，久美子展现了极佳的肺活量！“痛不欲生般的不甘心”前面那段非常棒。</blockquote>
肺活量是吹奏乐的基础，确实有些时候只看肺活量的水平就能看出一定的实力差距了，比如第五话全团绕操场跑圈，最突出的就是明日香和高坂，非常擅长运动的感觉，体现肺活量的强大，对她们的吹奏有很大帮助吧。 <blockquote>石原：演奏场景开始后就只是一个劲地演奏了，所以登台前的场景令人印象深刻。舞台旁的久美子与秀一，以及之后与明日香的交谈。

山田：我的话果然还是演奏场景。为了让这部分不光只是单纯的演奏场景，在演出时贴近了角色的心情。对一路观看下来的观众而言，这里的每一个镜头都应该会让人有所感触。</blockquote>
哈哈，丽奈solo的时候我全程都在看优子和香织的表情，太有意思了，尤其是优子，一脸的不爽又心服口服。

####  老贝

####  结标淡希  
##### 11505#       发表于 2015-8-7 15:12




所以虽然有突然冒出一句“爱的告白”、两人的脸贴得很近——这种令人心跳加速的描写，但久美子与丽奈是在精神上结合的两人。在我看来，比起含羞对视，还是“爱的告白”这种直截了当的发言更清爽纯洁。现实世界中如果有这样的朋友一定很不错。


所以说，这是精神色情片啊，比卖肉不知高到哪去了







-----

####  结标淡希  
##### 11506#       发表于 2015-8-7 15:15




县祭上秀一与叶月。这段剧情在原作第一卷中并未描写，之后发表的短篇中通过其他视点描述了这段约会，我们取了其中的要素。还有吹双簧管的铠冢霙这名角色，从第二集开始就悄悄出现在画面中，最终回加入了泷老师看着照片说“出发吧”的场景，获胜后明日香看上去并不怎么高兴的表情，这些不读原作第二卷以后的内容就无法明白。我们尽可能将原作中描写的要素反映到动画中。关于明日香在最终回中的表情，动画确实可以换一种描写，更痛快地收尾，可如果明日香在取得金奖后高呼“太好啦！”——这样欢天喜地的话，读过原作的人一定会觉得别扭。原作还有后续，但作为一部动画也想让它干净漂亮地收尾，我陷入过这种左右为难的困境。虽说如此，最终还是营造出了她们的故事仍将继续的气氛。

<img src="https://static.saraba1st.com/image/smiley/face/149.gif" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">最后一句非常微妙啊.....







-----

####  7450  
##### 11507#       发表于 2015-8-7 15:20



<blockquote>　　我想描写的久美子与丽奈的关系，是那种“男人之间的钦慕”般的感觉。我觉得她们是相互认同的竞争对手。“这家伙好帅”——久美子对丽奈怀着这样一种钦慕。这也是本作的主题之一。至今为止总是不知不觉地在随波逐流中走到现在的女孩子，通过邂逅另一个帅气的女孩，从而产生了自己也想与帅气的女孩一同前往同一个地点的愿望。由此拉开主人公成长故事的序幕，在我心中《吹响悠风号》就是这样一个故事。

　　久美子最早将丽奈视为“特别”的契机，是第八集丽奈的“爱的告白”。从那时起到第十二集为止的期间内，久美子逐渐产生了这样一种想法——要想与高远的丽奈并驾齐驱，那么自己也必须到达那个高度。久美子“想要演奏得更好”的原因之一，就是想与能提升自己的丽奈前往同一个地方，这个理由非常纯粹而美妙。所以虽然有突然冒出一句“爱的告白”、两人的脸贴得很近——这种令人心跳加速的描写，但久美子与丽奈是在精神上结合的两人。在我看来，比起含羞对视，还是“爱的告白”这种直截了当的发言更清爽纯洁。现实世界中如果有这样的朋友一定很不错。</blockquote>

这段说的好棒

####  alerbe  
##### 11513#       发表于 2015-8-7 17:21




——拥有60多人的北宇治高中吹奏乐部，从名字开始，制作组为每一个成员都做了设定，为何要做到这种地步？


　　因为想描写群像剧。但还是因为人数太多，实在难以将全员描写到位。系列构成的花田十辉也说过“如果可以的话，真想让每个成员都说句台词”。不过为了表现出角色的存在感，台词的语言也有讲究。先是音响导演鹤冈阳太指出了“高中女生说话会这么有条不紊吗”。比如一般作品中的台词会写得合乎逻辑、有条有理，但这次系列演出山田尚子组织了更符合高中女生风格的随意的对话。山田非常擅长组织女孩子的谈话，所以请她将台词调整为“符合高中女生风格的对话”。后期录音时，常常会发现一些不符合高中女生风格的有条不紊的对话，这时山田就会当场修改。画面中那些手和脚的可爱动作也得益于山田的演出。通过这部作品我再次感受到，她虽然身为女性，但真的好喜欢女孩子，好喜欢高中女生啊。

####  eaglet_loki  
##### 11526#       发表于 2015-8-8 01:09



 本帖最后由 eaglet_loki 于 2015-8-8 01:10 编辑 

前景很不明朗，石原果然是暂时燃尽了，把想做的都做了，这一季的主旨是“未成熟的主角与伙伴们为了实现一个目标而努力并成功”。


小说后面的内容比较难构成这样一个清晰的思路了，系列构成的难度变得很大。

当然不排除完全原创，那就要交给山田了，再来个爱情故事？

####  alerbe  
##### 11527#       发表于 2015-8-8 02:19



<blockquote><a href="httphttps://bbs.saraba1st.com/2b/forum.php?mod=redirect&amp;goto=findpost&amp;pid=29792818&amp;ptid=1085129" target="_blank">eaglet_loki 发表于 2015-8-8 01:09</a>

前景很不明朗，石原果然是暂时燃尽了，把想做的都做了，这一季的主旨是“未成熟的主角与伙伴们为了实现一个 ...</blockquote>
故事让他们改成这样，原作最后bg的结局是不可能再改回去了，故事的篇幅就不够。本身原作写的时候就有问题，秀一的内容太少，最后是强行结局，硬拧的比较难看。







-----

####  dxxtiger  
##### 11528#       发表于 2015-8-8 04:54




小说结局不论什么党都觉得难看，百合党感觉莫名起码吃到一口屎，BG党觉得完全是被机械之神吊起来的根本没有打赢的实感。小说整个剧情结构有点太散了，像是说了一大堆“配角”的故事突然想起来要给主角的感情路线一个交待于是三卷末赶紧结局，然后自己又觉得太生硬在四卷短篇里加塞。


其实个人觉得反正不只是主角，配角也已经和原作产生较大出入，而原作又可以说没有动画的开播很多人也不会去看，并没有多少真正意义上的“原作党”，真拍后续的话也可以继续脱离原作了。

####  alerbe  
##### 11543#       发表于 2015-8-8 20:17



[http://comic.qq.com/a/20150701/034574.htm](http://comic.qq.com/a/20150701/034574.htm)


Q：从音乐的角度来看，山冈小姐其实也可以在工作当中唱歌吧……


A：这个啊，声音跟乐器还是完全不同的呢。虽然我很擅长吹小号，但如果问我唱歌如何，那还是……（笑）我虽然明白音阶跟节奏，但身体并非就能够跟随这些要求来表现了……（笑）


Q：那么，就因为这些传言，所以山冈小姐才得到了优子的角色？


A：这个该怎么说呢（笑）。不过优子酱跟我一样，都是一个非常崇拜前辈的角色呢。并且她最喜欢的前辈·中世古香织是由茅原实里小姐出演的，而我也非常喜欢她本人！还有，优子吹的小号很偶然地跟我一样，都是银色。


另外，动画里面她参加了一个名为Sunfes的活动，并且那个时候优子拿着小号的动作也跟我很像哦。我自己都吓了一跳（笑）。


Q：这就是同步了吧（笑）。


A：我们的性格也非常接近呢（笑）。


Q：有时候看你们俩的照片，感觉总有些相似呢。


A：啊，可能因为我们都是黑长直的关系，有些不容易区分吧。有时候也会被人说很像呢（笑）。我们拥有的东西都很类似哦。比如说在京都都穿着有星星图案的衣服，在浅草玩的时候也很偶然穿了略有色差的鞋子。哦哦~！（笑）


Q：兴趣很相似嘛？


A：这个啊，倒是没觉得相似得多夸张。所以我跟我妈妈聊天的时候觉得更像是“前世的双胞胎”（笑）。


Q：那么在一起的时候，你觉得种田小姐有哪些优点呢？


A：这个恐怕得说上1个小时了（笑）。总之，她是个很直率的人。看起来非常老实，不过实际上很能迎合别人，另外也有一些天然的地方。恐怕我们俩的波长比较相近呢。去年在我生日的时候，她预约了一家餐厅，用来给我做精细哦。今天带着的手镯也是种酱在生日的时候送我的，我一直戴着。她可是专门去研究石头的效果，然后精心选择一个适合我的款式哦。而种酱也有个颜色不一样的款，但却是一对儿。所以绝对不能丢了（笑）。



我觉得要是出二期的话， 希美这个角色90%会选种田

####  心之渊  
##### 11559#       发表于 2015-8-9 15:08



<blockquote>心脏发出讨厌的声音跳动了一下，久美子屏住呼吸，只是看着丽奈的脸，尖锐的视线连向久美子，那纤细的手指紧紧地握紧了久美子的手腕。


冰冷的声音让久美子迅速脱开身子，跟着动作，小皮鞋踩踏砂子、鞋底摩擦了一下地面，久美子像是要逃避似的从那瞳孔中将视线避开，吹过的风狠劲地拍打在久美子的脸上。


久美子的视线彷徨于空中，她的手指透过衣服深入向久美子的皮肤，桃色的指甲点点地反射着室外电灯的灯光。总觉得感到苦闷，久美子不禁吐了口气，漏出的吐气中私自夹杂着自己的声音。

“因为我不想伤害到你。”

丽奈咽了咽口水，描绘着圆滑曲线的喉咙微微颤动着，她用指尖在久美子的手上比划着、困恼地叹了一声气，那手指的冰凉，让久美子颤颤发抖。

“这我我知道。”

丽奈垂着眼。

“即便如此我也希望你能告诉我。”

“.....抱歉。”

对于久美子的话、丽奈微微地摇了摇头，没事的、这么说着的她突然爬起来身，那张脸家上沾着数根黑发，久美子悄然地伸出手指，将那些个发丝拂开，被久美子触碰着脸、丽奈静静地垂下眼皮，那睫毛颤动了一下。

“我啊、对于自己的弱小吓了一跳，在听到有妻子的时候，受到了十分大的动摇。”

“受到动摇是想当然的啊、我也是被狠狠吓了一跳呢。”

“但是、我（原本）想着自己是个更加坚强的人。”

那么说着、她咬紧了嘴唇，久美子悄悄地将她那陷入沉寂的身子抱入怀中，与外界空气所接触的制服冰冰凉、只有她吐露的气息稍稍地在孕育些热量。</blockquote>

原作者病的比京阿尼严重多了

为什么不按时服药，要放弃治疗<img src="https://static.saraba1st.com/image/smiley/carton/164.gif" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

-----

####  alerbe  
##### 11563#       发表于 2015-8-9 16:30



<blockquote><a href="httphttps://bbs.saraba1st.com/2b/forum.php?mod=redirect&amp;goto=findpost&amp;pid=29806348&amp;ptid=1085129" target="_blank">结标淡希 发表于 2015-8-9 15:52</a>

病成这样子到底为什么会强行BG的


如果真的有二期的话这又是一段登山殒命（ ...</blockquote>
武田感觉就是想到哪写到哪，重点不突出到出扔闪光弹，最后强行收bg线完全无视之前几乎完结的剧情，不知道是谁的锅。 京都改编之后，几个反响突出的话，第八话登山有改动，演出强化，10和11话的故事走向完全不同，11话基本就是原创，包括夏纪和优子的关系被提前进化，13话的演奏部分的精彩也是文字体现不出来的。实际上原作只能说搭好了一个不错的框架，很多改动最后都是花田等人搞出来的。

####  Archlich  
##### 11617#       发表于 2015-8-12 00:48




ともよ様太能演了，以至于令人感到如同nico上的某条留言般：演已经是她血液的一部分，从超成熟的待人接物到陪着parunyasu等人胡闹，都有一种“兴奋的面具”的感觉。唯一能确定的是她真的很喜欢音乐。


借用丽奈的台词：想把那层皮扒掉看看！但不消说我们，她身边的人估计也很难有机会。


这大概也是最迷人的地方！

####  结标淡希  
##### 11689#       发表于 2015-8-15 12:56



<blockquote>回到一年级的房间，部员们开始更换衣服，在只有女生的房间里是没有“羞耻”这一概念存在的，大家都按照所喜好的样子随意地凌乱脱着，对于就这样穿着内衣阔步走着的同级生，久美子不禁笑了起来。

“啊、那个胸罩好可爱！”

“对吧对吧？今天可是决胜内衣啊。”

“那种不知道有没有的欧派、谈何决胜？”

“吵死人了！这就是所谓的讨个好彩头，为了能让学姐他们拿到金奖，穿来了关西大赛那会儿的胸罩。”

“靠你的胸罩来改变结果、谁能接受得了啊？”

“真是的！像这种，心情才是比较重要的。”

B组的成员开展着傻瓜似的的对话，在离着稍微有些距离的地方，丽奈打量着裙子的长度，像将膝盖埋在下面这种程度是在正赛时候的基准长度。黑红色的裙子底下露出她那修长的腿，在腿肚子和腿肚子之间所做出的缝隙间，久美子瞥了一眼那光滑的曲线然后轻轻拍了一下丽奈的肩膀。

“感觉怎么样？”

“还可以、吧。”

丽奈一如既往地摆着清澈的表情回答道，那视线停留在久美子的肩上。

“久美子、我给你绑个头发怎么样？”

“哎、为什么？”

“好了啦好了啦。”

丽奈强行让久美子往榻榻米上坐了下来，夹杂着鼻歌，开始用梳子梳起久美子的头发，在正赛，头发长的学生们都要将头发梳成一束，这是为了不给看的人留下不舒服的感觉。

“我啊、今天的正赛会加油的。”

丽奈的手指触碰到耳朵感到痒痒的，将有特点的头发好好梳理，用黑色的发夹夹住落下的剩余部分。

“solo啊、是个重要角色呢。”

“但是、稍微可能有点在紧张呢。”

那样说着，她停下了一次手，久美子回过头来，结果丽奈被惹生气地说道“别动”

“对于泷老师来讲这次的正赛也是重要的，那样想着，总觉得失败了的话不知道怎样才好。”

“没关系的哦。”

像是要打断丽奈说的话、久美子强力地断言道。

“丽奈的话是办得到的。”

因为是丽奈啊、对于久美子的话，丽奈冲破空虚似的，她陷入了数秒的沉默，然后受不了似的叹了口气，那柔软的双手抱住了久美子的脸颊。

“那是不能成为理由的。”

“会成的。”

“不会成的。”

对于撅着嘴的久美子，丽奈喉咙震动着、愉快地笑起来。

“那么、接下来轮到久美子绑我的头发了呢。”

“哎、我也要？”

“拜托了哦。”

那么说着、她就在久美子的跟前坐下，将长长的脚伸直、就像个小孩子似的朝这边伸出头，那是顺直没有歪斜的头发。在那之上穿过梳子，丽奈感到舒畅似的闭上了眼睛，怎么说好、仿佛就像猫咪一样。一边想着那些，久美子将手指滑向带有光泽的头发。</blockquote>


<img src="https://static.saraba1st.com/image/smiley/face/77.gif" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">你们秀恩爱考虑过群众感受吗！赶紧去结婚！不要给秀一留下任何机会！

####  结标淡希  
##### 11705#       发表于 2015-8-17 07:32



<blockquote>乐器搬运完毕、打击乐音部和其他的音部开始分开行动，将乐器从乐器箱子里取出、久美子周密地确认了一下有没有不妥。在那身旁正在组装双簧管的霙稍稍用了些带有得意的口气向这边搭话 。

“今天是最棒的簧片。”

那脸颊少有地泛着红潮，可以知道她虽然面无表情，但霙比平时来的要更加兴奋。

“是那样么？”

“嗯、是珍藏货。”

对于木管演奏者来讲、簧片是非常重要的，市场上贩卖的簧片有称心的也有不称心的，演奏者好像会从那其中仔细斟酌然后珍惜地使用称心的，尽是使用相同的簧片当然是马上会消耗完的，所 以好像都会在手边准备好几个上好的簧片、一点点地去习惯吹那个并且去使用它。因为金管乐器的号嘴没有消耗品，所以久美子对那方面的事情不是很了解，但是一考虑到这么小的零件所带来的影响，就感慨到乐器这种东西当真是复杂的构造啊。

“稍微有点砰砰直跳、solo，会不会有问题呢？”

“没事的啦、学姐在正赛上不是没出过失误么？”

“但是，全国大赛还是头一遭。”

就连霙学姐也紧张着、久美子考虑着理所当然的事，因为无论在哪个大赛上，她都面无表情挺胸抬头地吹奏乐器、所以肯定以为她是不会有那种感觉的人。

“我也是、砰砰直跳、但是，可能是高兴的那方面。”

“高兴的那方面？”

“是的、能在梦想中的舞台上进行演奏、超期待的。”

“那么、我也是。”

那么说着、霙洒落出腼腆的笑容，浅桃色的唇隙间露出洁白的牙齿。

“是金奖的话、就会受到希美的表扬了，所以、我会加油的。”

“那、那样啊？”

“嗯。”

还是老样子，她的世界好像是以希美为中心旋转着，但是、能孕育出那么优美的音色，久美子想着吹乐器的动机怎样都好。

“加油吧。”

那么说着霙就这么面无表情地朝这边伸出拳头，她采取这样的行动是挺少有的，面对不知所措的久美子，霙淡淡地告之。

“优子她、是在正赛前这么做的。”

久美子表示很接受她所说的话，确实、优子的话好像很喜欢这样的行为，让别人一直保持同样的姿势也是很失礼的，久美子将自身的拳头轻轻喷上霙的拳头。

“哼哼、”

虽然不知道是中了什么下怀，但霙表现出一副大悦的样子，看着那些，总感觉拉紧的力气也松弛了下来，相对于不禁大咧地笑起来的久美子，霙还是老样子面无表情。</blockquote>

希美控小天使。四天王里两个solo都持有“为你吹奏”技能，要是有第三个说不定全国大赛就能拿金了（

####  心之渊  
##### 11798#       发表于 2015-8-19 23:30




池田阿姨的staff日记，又要准备买日历了<img src="https://static.saraba1st.com/image/smiley/face/06.gif" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

===================


重谈悠风号☆クリス


クリス 2015年08月18日


〖原题目为まだユーフォ渍け，难以翻译〗


〖注:根据查找，池田晶子在之前已经写过了一篇有关悠风号的日志〗


最近重温了一下我5月时记录的anibaka〖即STAFF日志〗。虽然是这么说，但是从上个月开始我就一直在进行悠风号的周边设计。毕竟再有一个星期小学的暑假就结束了，所以现在孩子的作业进展也十分需要关注。〖池田晶子是4个孩子的母亲〗


今年和往年的夏天没有什么区别，不过，制作明年的日历时需要一些插图。日历，需要用复数张纸绘成插画后进行拼接。所以，关于这个日历中插画的相关事项我也非常认真地与商业部门进行了沟通。


这次本篇的制作已经结束了，一共绘出了7张日历图，不过到现在为止我仍旧沉浸在悠风号的美好氛围之中。


话说今年10月31日的活动信息已经详细公开了吧！今年也有很多人期待，我们正在锐意准备中&gt; &lt; 一定要为秋游京都做好准备呦♪

####  xsk120  
##### 11809#       发表于 2015-8-20 11:20



 本帖最后由 xsk120 于 2015-8-20 11:21 编辑 

渣翻渣听力。。。。有错记得指出，谢谢~


５

梨子：好久没有三个人一起去蛋糕自助餐了吧，优子夏纪

优子：最近没什么休息啊

夏纪：是啊，和去年完全不一样

梨子：这不是好事么，那么赶紧进店门吧

夏纪：好像很开心啊


店员：欢迎光临，请随便挑选自己喜欢的座位

梨子：夏纪优子，去哪边的座位？

夏纪优子：窗边！

优子：不要学我！

夏纪：我才要这么说

梨子：行行行，窗边就是了


优子：今天要吃到饱！

夏纪：会胖哦

优子：多的部分运动掉就行了！

夏纪：谁知道呢

优子：你才要注意呢，吃胖了可不管你

夏纪：我可是不会吃胖的体质，不用你关心

优子：。。。。。。。（拟声词就不用了吧）

梨子：嘛嘛，你们两个，一起去拿蛋糕吧。

夏纪优子；好~


梨子：这家店的蛋糕相当美味，不知不觉就会吃多了，你们说是吧？

优子：这是我的！最后一个了就让给我好了，我为了这个水果蛋糕才来的

夏纪：不要，你等等补充不就好了

优子：为什么要我等！你等等不就好了

夏纪：不要，不可能！

优子：什——么——！

梨子：话说回来，第一见面就是这样了啊


一年级的春天，在小卖店买午饭的时候

优子：这个炸猪排三明治是最后一个了，我想要~

夏纪：所以呢？

优子：让给我

夏纪：不要

优子：让给我也没什么吧

夏纪：只有你我才不要

优子：。。。。。。。。（拟声词）

梨子：嘛嘛，你们两个


夏天社团活动拍集体照片的时候

优子：为什么是你在香织前辈的旁边啊！一般不应该和我换么！

夏纪：就算你这么说我也不知道啊，只是你运气不太好。

优子：香织前辈的旁边一定是我！这是既定事项！

夏纪：这个在几月几号星期几，地球转了几圈的时候决定的啊？

优子：这个谁知道啊！香织前辈就是这么决定的！

夏纪：这你不是还没出生么

梨子：嘛嘛，你们两个


秋天的体育祭上社团对抗2人3足项目上

梨子：夏纪！优子！加油！

广播：啊，吹奏部的中川和吉川组合好快！还在加速！

夏纪：话说你能不能别跟着我！

优子：你才是别干扰我！

夏纪优子：啊——————

广播：优胜！吹奏部！大会新纪录！

优子：我跑的比你快！

夏纪：不是，是我！

夏纪优子：裁判！录像判断呢！

梨子：嘛嘛，你们两个


冬天去初次参拜的时候

优子：太好了！大吉！

梨子：太好了优子

优子：梨子呢？

梨子：我的是中吉，挺普通的。夏纪呢？

。。。。。。。

梨子：嗯？

夏纪：大凶。。。。

梨子：诶！！大凶？！

优子：。。。。（拟声词）大凶什么也太惨了哦~~~

夏纪：我从现在开始往上升就是了，你就只能往下了

优子：才不会往下呢，因为我是好孩子~

夏纪：自己说自己是好孩子，好冷~

优子：冷是因为你抽了个大凶吧~

夏纪：这才没有什么关系

梨子：嘛嘛，你们两个


梨子：为什么两个人这么意气相和呢，我一直都是在说：“嘛嘛，你们两个”啊

夏纪优子：啊！！

优子：这个是最后的水果蛋糕

梨子：啊，抱歉，有点发呆了

优子：梨子什么错都没有，说到底还是因为你妨碍我了

夏纪：被妨碍的是我吧

梨子：嘛嘛，你们两个，不要吵架了，3个人一起吃吧

夏纪优子：梨子和我两个人一起吃吧

夏纪：哈？

优子：哈？

夏纪：我和梨子一起吃！

优子：不不，我才要和梨子一起吃

夏纪：同样是低音组，我应该优先

优子：和这个没什么关系吧！

夏纪：有关系！

优子：这个在几月几号星期几，地球转了几圈的时候决定的啊？

夏纪：这个谁知道，从入部的时候开始！

优子：我不也是一起入部的！

梨子：嘛嘛，你们两个

夏纪优子：梨子你别说话！

优子：话说能不能别模仿我！

夏纪：我才要这么说！

梨子:。。。。。。（笑声）

夏纪：梨子？

优子：笑什么呢？

梨子：我觉得你们两个关系还真是好啊

夏纪优子：关系才不好！

####  RP城的老B样  
##### 11836#       发表于 2015-8-21 14:57



 本帖最后由 RP城的老B样 于 2015-8-21 15:32 编辑 

都这么久了还没人搬那个drama cd的久美子和丽奈篇么……微博上看到有人翻，我手打一份放这里算了。

于夏天的归途


在临近大赛的时候，我碰壁了。流畅吹出复杂乐谱的明日香学姐和吹不出的我。


在因为吹奏练习不顺而感到焦虑的某个夏天的归途中。


久美子：好热……都这么晚了还这么闷热。

丽奈：夏天的话很正常吧。

久美子：话是这么说……啊！！是石蛾！！（扑到丽奈身上的声音）

丽奈：……久美子？怎么了这是。

久美子：对不起……我很害怕石蛾。那长长的触须和毛毛的外形还有刺耳的声音让我从小时候起就觉得不舒服……光是想起来就心头发颤了。

丽奈：虫子什么的无视不就好了。

久美子：这算是冷笑话吗？（“虫子”和“无视”在日文中读音是相同的）

丽奈：啊？只是给你建议而已。

久美子：哈哈……说的也是呢，丽奈怎么可能会说那种大叔式的冷笑话……啊又是石蛾！！（又是扑到丽奈身上的声音）

丽奈：嘻嘻，你还真是容易被吓到的样子呢。

久美子：真是的，不要笑啦。

丽奈：因为这样的久美子很有趣啊。

久美子：哪有啊！我很平凡吧。THE 平凡。完全跟有趣扯不上关系的高中女生。

丽奈：明明会躲在自己房间跟植物聊天。

久美子：等等等等！为什么丽奈会知道这种事！

丽奈：配发简介册的时候出现的瞳同学告诉我的。

久美子：啊……那时候的那位啊。

丽奈：对。那时候我就在想，久美子果然是很有趣的人。

久美子：这算哪门子的有趣啊？不会被当成怪人吗？

丽奈：怪人？这么说好像也没错。

久美子：没错什么啊！

丽奈：想象一下你和植物聊天的样子，感觉很可爱呢。

久美子：可爱……？

丽奈：嗯。

久美子：哪里可爱啊？

丽奈：具体哪里可爱……一时也说不上来呢。

久美子：那不就是没有嘛……

丽奈：总之就是很可爱，是在夸你。

久美子：真是谢谢你啊。

丽奈：不用谢。



久美子：说起来，丽奈你在家里是什么感觉的？

丽奈：很普通的过啊。没有植物可以聊天。

久美子：这个就别再提了好吗……

丽奈：嗯……听听音乐，一个人去看电影什么的吧……

久美子：一个人去啊？

丽奈：嗯，一个人。

久美子：没有跟你一起去的朋友吗？

丽奈：啊？

久美子：哇！哇！对不起！那个，不是说丽奈你孤僻，是说……那个……这个……对不起……

丽奈：别在意，我没有生气。

久美子：谢谢。那个，如果可以的话，下次看电影的时候，我们一起去吧？

丽奈：可以吗？

久美子：嗯！

丽奈：我知道了，很期待和久美子一起出去玩呢。

久美子：嗯！我也是！嘻嘻，总觉得今天丽奈心情很好的样子呢。

丽奈：有吗？

久美子：嗯！

丽奈：哪里看出来心情很好呢？

久美子：嗯……一时半会也说不上来呢，但就是有这样的感觉。

丽奈：久美子不也说不出来嘛。

久美子：抱歉抱歉。不过，我也一起变得开心起来了。

丽奈：太好了呢。因为久美子你最近练习很不顺利的样子……

久美子：啊……嗯。那个很复杂的地方啊，明明明日香学姐能很轻易的吹出来，我却不能顺利吹好，非常不甘心啊。

丽奈：不甘心啊，非常非常不甘心吗？

久美子：这个我是最近才一点点明白的。

丽奈：嗯。

久美子：被泷老师问“能不能吹好”，到现在都不能给出答复。

丽奈：嗯。

久美子：但是看着丽奈就觉得不能继续这样下去。

丽奈：嗯。

久美子：想要吹得更好。

丽奈：嗯。

久美子：嗯。丽奈，你现在也还是想变得特别起来吧？

丽奈：当然！我想要变得更特别！

久美子：是吗，我也放心了。

丽奈：为什么久美子你放心了啊？

久美子：没什么啦……



久美子：我们来比赛吧，终点就是那座桥。

丽奈：诶？等一下啊久美子，不要突然跑起来啊。

久美子：输的人要请吃冰淇淋哦！

丽奈：真是的！我可不会输哦！

（跑步的声音）

久美子：诶！！好快！

丽奈：我本来就跑得很快啊，忘记了吗？

久美子：啊啊还真忘了！

丽奈：久美子，石蛾。

久美子：咦？呀啊！！

丽奈：先走一步啦~

久美子：啊啊被超过了！！真狡猾啊怎么这样子！

丽奈：快一点啦久美子！

久美子：丽奈你快得过头了啦~~~



久美子：距离大赛只剩下一点点时间了，我感到自己因为丽奈的话似乎能向前更进一步，在大赛那个闪耀的舞台上，吹出更多的声音。在这夏天的归途中，我这么想着。


久美子：那个，丽奈。

丽奈：嗯？

久美子：大赛，要赢哦。

丽奈：嗯。

####  tenjou

日文渣，翻了段最短的，话说拉拉是怎么知道久美子对植物说话的？这情报网强大得，莫非搭上了麻美子姐姐？


ララ、聞いちゃいました!その5
“拉拉，听说了”之5

叶月：诶，真的有各种各样的人呢，吹奏部
绿：绿，对接下来的社团活动变得期待起来了
久美子：哦？
叶月：因为(部员)类型丰富比较有趣嘛
绿：是啊，个性的碰撞产生新的音乐，简直是音乐的Big Bang(大爆炸)
久美子：个性吗，我没什么特别的个性呢

拉拉：拉拉，听说了！

久美子：已经……
绿：习惯了呢
叶月：嗯嗯

拉拉：黄前久美子酱似乎会跟自己房间里的观赏植物说话，烦恼的时候等等话尤其多哦。那么，拉拉就此(别过)。

久美子：啊啊啊啊啊啊啊，啊啊……
绿：久美子酱，个性，有的呢
久美子：诶？
叶月：真好呢，久美子
久美子：这样的个性，不要～～～

####  结标淡希  
##### 11857#       发表于 2015-8-22 09:25



 本帖最后由 结标淡希 于 2015-8-22 09:27 编辑 
<blockquote>就在进行着那些事儿的时候，泷受取了奖牌盾，久美子担忧地窥视着学姐他们，突然、丽奈站了起来，大家的视线集中于一点，她牢牢地抓住扶手，然后猛地吸了一口气，腹部挺起，能听见到呼吸声，那洁白的手指蕴含着力道，那娇嫩的嘴唇明确地动起来。

“我喜欢老师！”

会场内回响起丽奈的声音，小绿捂住自己的嘴角眼里放着光辉，叶月惊讶似的来回眨巴着双眼，泷一瞬间露出的惊讶般的表情，马上又在平日里的笑容中所散去，他朝二楼的观众席挥了挥手，行了一礼后走进了舞台里面。

“东京代表——”

表彰已经转向下一所学校，仿佛之前丽奈的告白不存在过一样，各个学校喊着各自的话语。

“丽奈？”

久美子拉了拉一直站在那的她的裙子一角，她的视线就这样凝于台上，无力地在那块地方坐了下来，雪白的脸颊上染上红色、眼瞳里晃动着泪花，平时清澈的表情不知道跑哪去了，从嘴唇里发出的叹息声向这边倾诉着她的动摇。

“怎、怎么办啊？久美子，我干了蠢事了，在这种地方告白什么的。”

那么说着、她用手心将自己的脸埋住，久美子连忙抓起她那手腕，<strong>不知为什么，现在更想看见她的那张脸</strong>。

“完全没事的哦。”

“不、但是、”

“还有、大家好像没认为那是告白来着。”

“哎？”

久美子的话让丽奈就这样睁大眼睛陷入了僵直，优子缓缓地从那背后靠近了过来。

“高坂、刚才真是出色的发挥啊、多谢啦。”

“哎？不、那是...”

“要是高坂不在的话想必大家谁都不会说些什么的吧，真是谢谢咯。”

那么说着，在背后的香织笑眯眯地笑着，恐怕丽奈的告白对部员们来说单纯的只是获得了声援。丽奈呆愣似的的盯着前辈们的脸，不久就摆出一副夹着安心和失落的表情说着“哪里哪里”摇了摇头。大概、泷老师也没察觉到丽奈的真心吧。

想着那些事情，久美子将视线转向舞台。

“总感觉是似失落似安心的心情啊。”

那么说着、丽奈好似害羞地挠了挠脸。

“丽奈你喜欢老师？”

将那悄悄低声耳语的小绿的侧腹，叶月轻轻地戳了一下，现在那种事就算了吧，那句话让小绿心不甘情不愿地点了点头。

“接下来、转向公布结果。”

对于那句话，喧闹的会场一瞬间回归寂静，丽奈将那表情绷紧，再次从扶手的缝隙间窥视台面上。</blockquote>
丽奈依然是个不管不顾的天然呆孩子啊....小黄又无意识吐槽伤人了。顺便99真的是个坏心眼痴汉啊（

####  7450  
##### 11870#       发表于 2015-8-24 10:32



<blockquote>“久美子、坐一块儿吧。”

那么说着、丽奈朝这边走进过来，嗯、久美子直白地点了点头。

“好累、可能会在公交车内睡着也说不定。”

“我也是，今天有点疲劳呐。”

二人边进行着那样的对话，边开始悠闲地走起来，在那相当靠前的地方，小绿和叶月朝着公交车奔了过去，别摔跤了、被梨子这样告诫着。

“高坂同学、”

突然搭过来的声音让久美子他们回过头，一看，泷正微笑着面向这边，在那身旁不知为何笑嘻嘻地露出愉快的笑容的明日香也在。

“啊、是的。”

认识到声音的主人的瞬间，丽奈的脸上染上了红色，泷一边拿着获得的奖牌盾一边不好意思地挠了下头。

“颁指挥奖的时候，给我搭上话真是谢谢了。”

“哪、那里，我并没有做什么值得道谢的事。”

发出“嗡嗡”的声音一般，丽奈大力地摇了摇头。长长的马尾前端好几次顺着打在了久美子的脸上，是太过高兴了么、丽奈没有注意到那种事，着着那个，明日香越发地憋住好笑的笑容。绝对是在找着乐子啊、想着那些久美子将视线转回到泷那边。

“说老实话，由于稍微有些没自信，（能说那些）真是让我感到高兴。”

“自信？什么自信？”

久美子的质问让泷苦笑起来。

“来到这个学校后，我自我感觉并不是一味地被大家所喜欢，不安地想着自己是否在自以为是地进行着指导，莫非自己难道不是只是在强推给学生们自己想做的事.....”

“才没有那样的事！”

像是要打断泷的话一般，丽奈喊了起来，泷一瞬间惊讶似的睁大了眼睛，然后静静地微笑。

“能有这样给出否定的学生在，我真是幸福呢。”

“并不是只有我，大家也一定都尊敬着泷老师，一开始可能会有稍许有些道出不满的人在，但是现在大家都对老师报以感谢，呐、久美子？”

突然间被要征求同意，久美子一个劲地点了点头，丽奈就这样面红耳赤，然后和泷的距离靠近了一步，那眼瞳，现在也尽是垂落地睁大开，她用力地握紧自己水手服的一角，然后一个劲地说道。

“我、喜欢老师，选择北宇治也是因为有老师在，所以，那个、我真的是很喜欢老师。”

“能得到那样的话，很庆幸能当上老师呢，谢谢了。”

那么说着，泷和蔼可亲地微笑起来，那个反应，让在旁边观望两人对话的明日香和久美子看了看对方的脸，这个老师绝对是没有明白。

但是告白的当事人被道谢后却摆出副幸福的面孔，嘛、丽奈感到满足的话就行了，想着那些，久美子透过玻璃将视线游走向会场内，直到先前还挤满一堆人的会场现在也相当平静了下来，就像到先前为止的热闹气氛都是骗人的一样，之前所发生的事不全都是梦么？就是有着那样的感觉。</blockquote>
<img src="https://static.saraba1st.com/image/smiley/face/08.gif" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

<blockquote>“在过道遇到进藤先生那边。”

久美子的话让泷回想到似的点了点头说道“是那样啊”

“然后，就被拜托给吹上低音号的人传个话。”

“传话么？”

明日香的眉头抽搐地动了一下，平时的扑克脸崩溃了，她的表情上游走着动摇，不知道有没有注意到那个，泷平稳地点了点头。

“‘好好坚持走到这步了呢，真是美妙的音色啊。’——就是那样，像这样从评委那得到赞赏的事情可是很少见的哦，是值得庆幸的呢。”

那句话让明日香屏住了呼吸，通过透明的镜片，能知道她的眼瞳里一晃一晃地摇曳着。

“是、那样么？”

明日香回味似地呢喃道，只是静静地垂下眼皮，长长的睫毛碰撞在眼镜的镜片上，她的努力就凭那一句话就得到回报了吧，像要摸索她的心情一般，久美子抬头看向明日香的脸，是注意到了那视线了么，明日香的嘴角浮现出带有苦笑般的微笑，然后摸了摸久美子的头。

“真是的、吹上低音号的被夸奖了。”

“啊、是的，很开心呢。”

“我也很开心。”

那么说着、她露出洁白的牙齿笑了出来，那爽朗的笑容是久美子直到现在为止还没有看见过的东西，是兴奋着么、明日香没有停止抚摸，莫非、她是对率直的喜悦而感到害羞，可能才通过这么做来掩饰吧，即使头被粗暴地摇晃着，久美子也绝不会去制止，泷微笑地了望着那边的情况。

“抱歉、久等了。”

丽奈挥了挥手，从会场的入口处朝这边奔了过来，对于那个久美子也回过来招起手来，突然间明日香停下了手，直直地俯视着不禁回过头来的久美子的脸，两眼相交，仿佛就像被束缚一般，久美子在那个地方陷入了僵直，忽然、明日香拉近了距离。

由于她那整洁的脸蛋突然间靠近了过来，久美子一下子闭上了双眼，从她嘴唇中所泄露出来的气息，弄得久美子的耳朵瑟瑟发痒，在那耳边，明日香低声细语道。

“久美子你喜欢上低音号么？”

突然的提问让久美子无意识地迅速回答上来。

“是的、我喜欢。”

是对那个迅速的回答感到吃惊么、明日香一瞬间睁大了眼睛，从制服那无防备地所露出的喉咙愉快似地颤抖起来，她可疑地眯起眼来，轻轻地拍了下久美子的肩膀，什么也没有涂的手指甲闪闪地弹射出室外的灯光。

“哼哼、我也是。”

那样笑着的明日香如同年幼的孩子一般。</blockquote>

心疼明日香<img src="https://static.saraba1st.com/image/smiley/face/88.gif" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

这是历年成绩，2011-2014连县大赛都没有出场：

<img src="https://img.saraba1st.com/forum/201508/28/095858pkuussank56oae6s.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">


<strong>e0416818367adab466bff9298dd4b31c8601e4c2.jpg</strong> (0 Bytes, 下载次数: 0)

下载附件

2015-8-28 09:58 上传





精华女子高校常年在全国大赛拿金奖，因为有个很有名的顾问叫藤重佳久，但是藤重先生今年60岁从精华退休了，之后4月份来到了[长崎](http://jump.bdimg.com/safecheck/index?url=rN3wPs8te/pL4AOY0zAwhz3wi8AXlR5gsMEbyYdIw61guVtWYp62uRBIrhAk6Zc5t6XyibVFgk4fbLMgytUg5Z4Q4OO30Ri8SAtVjSx1NjJY8K44RtEayJ5MTaGJ3cpL/nOjfTHck+Fw26MNhlXb5ThNkx5eRCn5mTYQw9XtLoJE53KVHXKTrXoCaTHM8s8HXrW/TeIRjQgwPGbuJnYGNA==)県活水高等学校担任顾问。在藤重先生的带领下，活水高校吹奏乐部仅用4个月就拿到了全国大赛资格！
这个奇迹就像万年初战败退的[棒球](http://jump.bdimg.com/safecheck/index?url=rN3wPs8te/pL4AOY0zAwhz3wi8AXlR5gsMEbyYdIw60PuTi7FH6K6C8c2w72BJITt6XyibVFgk4fbLMgytUg5Z4Q4OO30Ri8SAtVjSx1NjJY8K44RtEayJ5MTaGJ3cpL/nOjfTHck+Fw26MNhlXb5ThNkx5eRCn5mTYQw9XtLoJE53KVHXKTrXoCaTHM8s8HXrW/TeIRjQgwPGbuJnYGNA==)部突然进入了甲子园一样让人震惊，飞跃速度绝对可以说是百年不遇，在业界引起了很大冲击，网上有人评价“真是像动画和电视剧情节一样的大飞跃，太震惊了！”

<img src="https://img.saraba1st.com/forum/201508/28/100839qygvq88j48lg4zyj.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

####  sakurawwt  
##### 12101#       发表于 2015-9-8 00:12



 本帖最后由 sakurawwt 于 2015-9-8 00:31 编辑 
<blockquote><a href="httphttps://bbs.saraba1st.com/2b/forum.php?mod=redirect&amp;goto=findpost&amp;pid=30090228&amp;ptid=1085129" target="_blank">xsk120 发表于 2015-9-7 21:26</a>

组团么23333</blockquote>
怎么组？ 

目前计划： 

北京10月31日出发 大阪落地入住 看情况 有时间就去京都30周年活动会场 没时间就去宇治爬夜山

11月1日 一早参加京都30周年活动 根据活动时间 或者宇治巡礼 或者 去京阿尼本部

11月2日 目前没计划 如果前两天时间紧张 就这天去巡礼 如果时间充裕就去电器街逛逛

11月3日 乘坐航班回家

没有太多假期 纯粹是为了活动 生挤出两天时间 目的很单一 


如果有兴趣 可以PW文文 

京阿尼30年活动参加卷需要提前网上预约
[http://kyoanido-event.com/en/](http://kyoanido-event.com/en/)

活动宣传CM
[http://www.bilibili.com/video/av2480025/](http://www.bilibili.com/video/av2480025/)

活动PV
[http://www.bilibili.com/video/av2823686/](http://www.bilibili.com/video/av2823686/)

京吹部的staff座谈在第二天（11月1日）

P3：【悠风号组谈小号组】明日香：一看到香织就流口水啊，女子力爆棚，看起来好好吃。【久美子、夏纪石化中】明日香：久美子不会吗？久美子：才不会！这种想法好吓人！明日香：那么丽奈酱的大腿呢？久美子：诶？口水。。。明日香：对夏纪来说那就得是优子了吧。久美子：啊咧？夏纪：想起优子流口水？真心不会啊。。。（这俩人是要闹哪样。。。）

P4【小号组谈悠风号组】香织：明日香好帅气，真是让人憧憬！丽奈：久美子是个怪家伙，不过挺有意思的。优子：夏纪？我干嘛要谈起她啊？夏纪就是个又爱作弄人、又孩子气、又不会看场合、说话恶毒、不修边幅的不良少女，总之就是讨厌讨厌讨厌讨厌。。。丽奈：这完全就是进入恋爱模式了嘛。【香织：我就笑笑不说话】优子：等一下，才不是！

P5【从明日香学姐重回吹部开始优子就好烦人】优子：人家想吃冰激凌！夏纪肯定也想吃吧？回家路上一起去吃嘛。夏纪：那个啥，莫非优子你很想跟我一起去？优子：谁~谁想跟你一起去啊！夏纪：果然是这样啊！铠塚：不去吃冰激凌么？希美：又开始了啊。夏纪：不管怎样优子就是超喜欢我的吧。优子：你！是要报复啊？【画面回放，铠塚小天使事件中】优子：你超喜欢我的吧。夏纪：哈？？无路赛！

P6优子：你这家伙有什么值得喜欢的？铠塚：优子很喜欢夏纪的哟。【夏纪优子石化中】
铠塚：因为，优子之前不是说“谁会跟讨厌的人在一起啊”？优子老是跟夏纪在一起啊，对吧？希美：确实，Mizore说的没错。铠塚：被希美夸奖了，希美×6。。。希美：那两个人明明心里清楚，但是一点都不坦率呢。铠塚：这样啊？【夏纪优子持续石化中】

####  tenjou  
##### 12170#       发表于 2015-9-12 20:28




复杂又可爱的谜步是由三好一郎设计的，先将舞步做成动画，然后发给原画师参考。被问及谜步好在哪里时，三好回答“谜步就美在谜上”。


----------------------

谜步的好就在于谜上！


还有那眼睛的高光，不讲解还真没注意到，只觉得特别水灵，原来还有这种门道，不愧是细节京！

####  心之渊  
##### 12200#       发表于 2015-9-15 16:11




搜到8月初的一个radio的内容


这周ラジオED稍微说到一点dramaCD内容，ともよ说作为久美子和丽奈的役者，她和安済印象最深的都是第11轨(夏の日、帰り道にて)。对于真正喜欢故事本身的人来讲意义比较不一样，也不同于其他描绘吹部有趣一面的音轨。应该是有说到8话之后及正式比赛前日两人的单独对话…她们也是怀着相当认真的心情去录的


ともよ说她在拿到剧本之前都小看了drama内容，因为是在最终话录完的燃尽状态下的第二周参加的drama收录，再加上本以为会是以配角为主场热热闹闹的小故事，没想到最后一轨竟然来这么一出……


另外3. 滝昇の特別な一日大概是滝卖萌回ww “没有眼镜的滝先生的一天”


朝井喜欢なかよし川那轨ww看了下标题感觉应该就是四卷那个小短片了……其实一开始以为帰り道也是……


repo by @駄話坂

####  静肃之怀刃  
##### 12228#       发表于 2015-9-15 23:35



<blockquote><a href="httphttps://bbs.saraba1st.com/2b/forum.php?mod=redirect&amp;goto=findpost&amp;pid=30170873&amp;ptid=1085129" target="_blank">starring 发表于 2015-9-15 23:01</a>

玉子简直美cry


秀一表示只要山田加BUFF，还能逆推一波</blockquote>
我趴在地上想了好久也实在想不出来秀一基怎么翻盘，我觉得动画一期里面秀一基的戏份已经比小说里多了不少了。

小说第二卷里跟秀一基有关的剧情我已经想不起来了，第三卷虽然专门有一章叫做“轰鸣吧！长号！”但是实际上秀一基的戏份也不多。

虽说短篇集最后一章是秀一基主场，但是之前也有好多人表示跟本篇三卷相比剧情跳跃太大，怀疑是作者为了世界和平强行发糖。


总而言之秀一基就去哭晕在厕所里吧，现在已经是两川的时代了。<img src="https://static.saraba1st.com/image/smiley/face/34.gif" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

“秀一这家伙是不是又长高了？”，“我为什么会期待秀一这家伙说什么，这家伙到底说不说啊”，“这样的距离，我要不要靠近一点。”

####  孤舟垂钓  
##### 12236#       发表于 2015-9-16 10:58




又一次看三年级诸位角色初期设定案，不得不佩服京都的勇气，那么多版本里选了最土的版本，虽然是很符合小城市普通高中的末流吹奏乐团，但是假如是一群帅哥美女，对宅男的吸引力一定会更大吧。

明日香初设好手冢，扁镜无框眼镜严肃脸，无敌的感觉。葵侧脸美如画，正脸灭丽奈。晴香经历了病娇少女-&gt;贵族少妇-&gt;双马尾毒舌-&gt;最终的地味和事老部长的一系列变迁，可谓诸位中定位变化的最大的。

####  心之渊  
##### 12254#       发表于 2015-9-16 14:45




8话的演出藤田春香祭典那天大雨也去爬山了2333，不知道圣地巡礼的fan有没碰到她，8话的staff们经常没事儿去爬个山

琥珀是小号的绿是山田的兴趣，之前山田有说过如果说最喜欢谁的话，就选琥珀好了（hentai

叶月和琥珀那段也是山田的主意的样子



藤田：久美子看着丽奈的发饰走路就像魔法解开一样

石原：这话是女性来做演出真是太好了，男性来的话会变的过于h

藤田：我有注意不让它变成这样，不是特意要制造这种感觉，而要保留角色最原本的感情，做最原本的演出这才是特别的吧



最烦恼的是丽奈的连衣裙颜色。两颗星星的象征是石原的主意

石原：我是比较在意月历和星星位置的人，偶尔这一天，看着模拟运行星星轨迹的软件，正好金星来到了个好位置，木星也在，在互相靠近

石原：一般来说不想让ed消失。这里向制作人请求了制作了这个特殊ed


repo by @灵然随想

-----

####  结标淡希  
##### 12268#       发表于 2015-9-16 17:53




再转一遍，这一段简直炸裂：[http://weibo.com/p/1001603855375895029806](http://weibo.com/p/1001603855375895029806)
 <blockquote>花火大会



“抱歉，让你久等了。”


久美子到达教室的时候，看到丽奈正背着书包默读着英语单词书。头脑聪明的孩子从不浪费时间呢——久美子深切地感受到了这一点。长长的睫毛缓缓地上扬，伏在其下的眼眸映出久美子的方向。静止不动的薄唇微微地缓和了一点。


“不，没有等多久。没关系。”


“是吗？那就太好啦。”


久美子拿起自己的书包，对着教室里的前辈说，“今天辛苦了”“辛苦了”，交换了问候之后，久美子和丽奈向着阶梯下走去。和她一起回家还是第一次，不知为何有点心跳加速。


“久美子你、12号的花火大会和谁一起去？”


（中略久美子说她不打算与秀一一起去）


长长的黑发别到耳后，丽奈面无表情地仰头看着天空。


“那，要跟我一起去吗？”


久美子不由地凝视着丽奈的脸。但是她并不往这边看。如同是在找什么借口一样，丽奈不停顿地快速说了下去。


“不是、如果有空的话不是挺好的吗，如果有空的话。”


黑发的间隙间可以看见形状优美的耳朵。看着平常白皙的皮肤染上一片朱红，久美子无意识眨了眨眼睛。


“难道说丽奈是在害羞吗？”


“不是，并不是这样的。”


她这么说，逃避般移开视线往旁边看去。这个反应实在太过好懂。久美子不由地笑出声，胸口有些发痒。听着她“哈哈哈”的笑声，丽奈红着脸看了过来。


“并不是特别习惯这种事！邀请什么的...！”


“是这样吗？”


“就是这样。”


“即使如此还是来邀请我了？”


听到这样的询问，丽奈轻轻敲打着久美子的背。


“不要这样得意地笑。”


“没办法啊。”


这样回答她，久美子才知道自己嘴边竟扬着这样的笑容。不知为何脚步变得轻快了。


“能收到邀请很开心，一起去吧。”


久美子话音未落，丽奈轻哼了一声。红色的水手服胸前摇动着白色的领巾。久美子将书包往肩上提了提，“呼呼”地小声轻笑着。






与丽奈相约见面的地方是宇治神社前。（具体风景描写请看动画第一集）环视着周围，还没有见到丽奈的身影。




“抱歉！稍微有点迟到。”


正向着神社内部眺望的时候，从后边传来了丽奈的声音。回过头，眼前站立着美得令人难以置信的少女。


渐变色的布料做成的深青色浴衣，大大的白色燕子交错飞舞，与明黄色的腰带相互映衬着色彩。长发向上绑起，被装饰着天然石的簪子固定住。仿佛是中从哪里的广告中飞了出来的一般。久美子的脸颊染上赤红。


“非常美丽呢，吓了我一跳。”


听到久美子这样笑着说，丽奈移开目光。


“没什么，才没有这种事。”


表情淡定地说出这句话的少女，耳后稍稍带了一点红色。久美子将视线移向鸟居，可以看见人潮涌动。花火大会即将开始的宣告声传来。丽奈握紧了久美子的手腕。


“差不多该过去了。”


“要在哪里看？”


“塔之岛。”




刚踏上朝雾桥，就传来了花火的声音。瑰丽的光芒在天空中升起，像是花朵绽放一般的色彩。鲜艳的红色伴着青光向四面八方散开。“啪啦啪啦”落在地上的，是光之鳞片。


“花火，似乎已经开始了呢。”


丽奈说。“嗯。”久美子同意道。在朝雾桥观看是禁止的。久美子与丽奈继续前进。到达浮岛，岛上有一座十三重塔，高约15米。是日本存在的最大的古石塔。




“久美子、想要吃什么吗？”


“嗯...苹果糖什么的。”


“我想吃刨冰。”


“刨冰也不错呐。”


这样的对话结束，结果是久美子把两种东西都买了。




走到了一个没什么人的地方，丽奈停下了脚步。


“嘛，这里就可以了吧？”


丽奈回过头问。久美子吃了一口苹果糖，真甜。


“刨冰小心不要掉下来了哦。”


“嗯，会注意的。”


丽奈开始吃自己的刨冰。放进嘴里，细细咀嚼。然后按紧了太阳穴。“头痛。”听到她这么说，久美子笑了笑。


“真是的，不要一口气吃下去啊。”


“很久没吃有点忘了。”


丽奈这么说，眉间轻轻皱起。


（然后开始聊第二卷的主线，聊到一半——）


丽奈说，嘴角向上扬起。被冰水濡湿的桃红色唇瓣闪着蛊惑人心的光辉。


（继续聊。丽奈说二年级退出的那些人只是在逃避而已，她自己绝对不会逃。）


“唔——很有丽奈风格的想法呢。”


“是吗？只是普通的看法吧？”




——逃跑。


这句话在久美子的脑子里回荡。久美子并不像丽奈那样强。退出部活这样的想法其实也有过好几次了。逃跑也不错吧，反正只是部团活动。如果这么说的话，丽奈的脸一定会涨得通红，会认真地发怒。丽奈一直都是这么认真。和自己，完全不一样。和这样容易受旁人流动所影响的自己。久美子向旁边看去。


在至今距离下，她的肌肤上依然一丝毛孔都看不到。花火的光芒映照之下，她的轮廓描出美丽的剪影。可以看到纤长的睫毛缓慢地上下眨动。从浴衣里露出来的锁骨上，滴落的汗水温柔地抚过。


丽奈感觉到久美子的视线，唇边绽开轻笑。一直都带着冷漠的眼瞳，在久美子面前变得温和。丽奈认为久美子是特别的。久美子也是、认为丽奈是特别的。这样的事突然让久美子害怕了起来。像是在薄冰上站立，这样的感觉。




映照在水面上的花火一瞬间散开。看着在夜空中盛开的、没有实心的花朵，丽奈感叹地叹息。


“真美啊。”


说着这样的话的她才是最美丽的那个，久美子想。


这样最喜欢的朋友若是以后分别了，还会再次见到吗？


久美子知道，友情从来不是永远的东西。中学时期每天见面的朋友，现在已经十分疏远了。如果这个瞬间可以放进容器里冷冻保存就好了。这样的话，就不会突然有这么害怕的感觉。




“丽奈、”


仿佛是织布时微小震动着一般的声音。听到久美子的呼唤，丽奈将头稍稍倾了过来。动起来的时候，发簪的装饰发出清脆的声响。


“嗯？怎么了？”


回答她的是这样温柔的声音，久美子惊慌了起来。甘甜的声音融进耳朵里，身体里的热量不断向脸上集中。没什么，什么都没有。这样的话无论如何也说不出来。不知该怎么做，久美子吃了一口苹果糖。酸甜的香气在口中散开，已经变成怎样都好的心情了。粉色的烟火在头顶盛开。轰鸣般的冲击音响彻耳际。




思考话题的时候，久美子不知为何安下心来。面上浮现出沉思的表情，丽奈看着她。


“那个啊，之前跟叶月和绿辉约好一起去泳池。丽奈你——”


“我去。”


她立刻回答。


“真意外。我还以为丽奈并不喜欢这样的事情。”


“这样的事情是指？”


“和许多人一起出去玩什么的。”


“啊啊，这种事情确实不是太喜欢。”


丽奈一边说着一边耸了耸肩。


“不过，去年买的泳衣、还非常的紧。今年怎么想也应该穿一穿了。也没什么去泳池的时机。”

“很紧什么的，难道说...”


“真是的，不要说下去了。”


她这么说，稍微有点害羞地轻轻敲打久美子的肩膀。看着包裹在布料里的丰满曲线，久美子不禁低头看了看自己......嗯，视野良好。有着这样的格差，神明大人还真是残酷呢。




“久美子穿着泳装的样子，真是很期待呢。”


丽奈微笑着说。




END




翻译上一篇的时候有很多人说不懂为什么作者要强行BG，我觉得这样说不太好...然而翻译这一篇的时候，我满脑子只剩下“作者你为什么要强行BG？！！！”


总之这两个人为什么还不去结婚！！！！！


另外，很明显可以看出来，除了痴汉丽奈这一点外，动画里的小黄同学已经跟小说里有很大的差别了，赞美京阿尼【</blockquote>


<img src="http://ww3.sinaimg.cn/mw1024/005BNtwogw1etwvwi10mqj30oc0xcqay.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">


后面炸开的那个就是我（

于是在叶月小绿以及已经毕业的前辈们的鼓励下

久美子向着机场奔跑而去

秀一回头看着那呆滞的眼光，小丑般圆润滑稽的脸庞无论看多少次都让人不由得从内心发出微笑。
噗嗤！
秀一发出了笑声，眼泪悄悄地从眼角流下。
“你是大号君，不是大号。谢谢你，不过我的答案是不会改变。可能现在，说不定以后久美子也不会改变心意，但是，现在我是不会放弃，也不想那么轻易放弃。所以，对不起，加藤。”
大号君的身体微微地晃动一下，一边笨拙地举起双手脱下头套，一边说道“抱歉我不是加藤，但是我对你刚刚那番话很好奇。”
………待续

都在婊秀一基，我来奶一下

####  心之渊  
##### 12416#       发表于 2015-9-22 03:53



 本帖最后由 心之渊 于 2015-9-22 04:09 编辑 

大半夜在撸第一话的监督音轨，石原老贼个死傲娇，感谢山田还要加一句我自己也可以2333


 京阿尼里面吹奏乐经验者有20来个


99自言自语的那一部分

山田：久美子是一位女孩子，是妹妹。所以我认为她是一位能察言观色的人

石原    我也认为她是这么生活过来的，我想作为次女差不多是看到姐姐被父母训斥里成长的

所以说弟弟或妹妹比较聪明或者说比较尖

山田　反过来说她们会刻意压抑自己不会明面说出自己的喜好。所以久美子的房间就会突出自己的喜好

石原   原来是这样啊这段的演出有这个意思

山田　太不信任我了，我认为妹妹都会有这种感觉

石原　确实，你说的我懂。确实很喜欢自己的房间这个说法


山田的姐姐吹上低音号的，小时候跟山田介绍的时候说比大号小一点，不过山田对大号那时候也没概念，姐姐的上低音号是银色的


石原老贼买了个悠风号的号嘴，上班还吹，不过吹不响233

高桥立刻吹出来了，而且说上低音号比小号好出声，让石原非常郁闷



京阿尼买了个很贵的上低音号做参考，和丽奈小号一起买的

####  心之渊  
##### 12436#       发表于 2015-9-22 18:24




高尾：为什么秀一会在中途的黄檗站上车，为了买面包中途下过车吗？

石原：不是为了买面包，买面包只是顺便。吹奏乐部的一年级男生只有两个人，所以秀一与吹萨克斯的泷川Chikao关系很好。他们经常一起回家，泷川在黄檗站下车，秀一也下车和他闲聊，顺便买面包吃。

高尾：Chikao在黄檗站下车，也就是说他不是特地（陪秀一）来到黄檗站的吧？

石原：他在黄檗站下车，然后再回到车站送别秀一。

高尾：啊，还有个问题，为什么丽奈也在此时出现，她也是从黄檗站上车的吗？

石原：丽奈并不是在那里上车的。

高尾：正好看见久美子于是就坐过去了？

石原：嗯，她应该原本就和久美子在同一辆电车中。

高尾：秀一回家时总是乘上久美子所在的那辆电车，那是偶然吗？

石原：应该是偶然吧。

高尾：我还以为秀一在等她呢。

石原：你要这么解释也可以。


黑泽：你们听我说，据说这里是Chikao离家最近的车站，Chikao和秀一去买面包，然后Chikao为了送别秀一特地买了张站台票回到这里。说到底这个车站离学校只有一站，Chikao恐怕不是乘电车通学的，他特地买了站台票为秀一送行。

樱井：真的假的啊Chikao！

黑泽：然后秀一连“Chikao，明天见”都不说一句就走了，你们想想被留下来的他是怎样一种心情！

寿：确实，这家伙……

樱井：就是那个吧，这时候女生就会开始讨论他们有一腿什么的，真让人气愤啊。



怎么感觉石原觉得基友才是真爱，tomoyo就觉得秀一是个负心汉23333<img src="https://static.saraba1st.com/image/smiley/face/26.gif" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

####  心之渊  
##### 12438#       发表于 2015-9-22 18:26




石原：虽然片中县祭当天没有下雨，但现实中那天下着雨。

藤田：没错，下得挺大的，县祭那天我去登大吉山了。

石原：县祭当晚？真的吗！我是之前取材的时候去的。

藤田：过程中与许多人擦肩而过，山顶也聚集了很多人，吃了一惊。画分镜前的冬天也和原画师一起去过一次，负责上色的大冢（芙由纪）也一个人去登过……为了在制作时能切身体会到剧本中描写的气氛，第八集的许多制作人员都自发去登山，令人深深感受到了大家对第八集的爱。

石原：本片的舞台离公司很近所以很方便，随时都能去取材。


8话的分镜去年冬天就做了？感觉开始好早

那今年京阿尼在干嘛<img src="https://static.saraba1st.com/image/smiley/face/09.gif" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

####  木宇水  
##### 12523#       发表于 2015-9-26 02:44



<blockquote>xsk120 发表于 2015-9-25 22:29
哎。。。LS的八成现在已经晚了，但是我还是要说一句，直接去JR宇治车站旁边的有个案内中心去领圣地巡礼图不 ...</blockquote>
我擦，车站还有这种宅地图……昨晚顺利的看到宇治桥，宇治川超级大一条而且水流很急，拍了下小黄哭着转弯跑到桥的景，也看到桥对面列车驶过。京吹的景好真实，刚好看到有学生妹身材不错而且水手服很好看比京吹还好看，感觉非常棒，哇咔咔。对了，是不是eva最后一部要出了，叫x，看到附近的液晶大屏在卖广告。卧槽的是，去宇治神社大吉山路上好静啊，没几个人啊建筑又那么古色古香……在宇治神社拍了下赶紧走，经过宇治上神社，已经关门了就没进去看，继续朝山上走。开始登大吉山……我就卧槽槽槽了，山路上没灯……没灯……没灯……知道为什么丽奈要装个手电筒app吗，因为没灯啊卧槽！！（原来京ani在委婉的表示宅们朝圣前要做好准备，现在懂了），这么晚登山心里那个荒呀（在木幡看大本营的小黄屋和附近作画室看晚了），想着来都来了就硬着头皮走上去了，因为看着google地图好像山路没多长，然而……事实证明我错了，原来显示的终点只是山腰……最终还是怂了……原路折回。因为其实要说夜景，在大阪的高楼看更漂亮吧应该。往下走拐弯处也看到一些夜景，蛮漂亮的。好啦，回去了。宇治车站旁边有家便利店，门外有扭蛋，跟小黄约丽奈出来的景好像，怀疑是不是就是那里取的景。可惜扭蛋没有乐器的，不然就来一发

哈哈~

####  心之渊  
##### 12571#       发表于 2015-9-29 21:58



 本帖最后由 心之渊 于 2015-9-29 22:01 编辑 

23号发行的fanbook之前有流出作者炸裂级的对谈内容

有老外翻译了其中花田的石原的访谈，英文应该会比较好懂，大家不妨一看

[https://ultimatemegax.wordpress. ... -hanada-translated/](https://ultimatemegax.wordpress.com/2015/09/28/sound-euphonium-interview-jukki-hanada-translated/)

这篇是花田的

<strong>Sound! Euphonium Interview: Jukki Hanada (translated)</strong>

This is the second of a series of interviews with various staff members of Sound! Euphonium that was published in the Official Fanbook released by Takarajimasha on September 23.

Series Composer:Jukki Hanada

Scriptwriter. Notable works include Beyond the Boundary, Love, Chuunibyou, &amp; Other Delusions, and Steins;Gate (series composer for all).

<strong>A scenario packed with the atmosphere of a concert band</strong>
<strong>– What impressions did you have after first reading the novel?</strong>

It was a very entertaining read. I was completely absorbed into the story as I read, especially with the power behind the last part with the showoff between Reina and Kaori for the solo. As I took notes for the scenario, I wondered if we would be casting too big a net with the number of characters we have for only 13 episodes, considering the number of people in a band is so huge. How we would narrow down our depiction of which characters was something I was aware of from the very beginning. In a novel, you aren’t concerned with characters that are around the protagonist if you don’t write about them, but you’ll see them in an anime.
<strong>– Did Director (Tatsuya) Ishihara give you any requests concerning how the scenario would go?</strong>

Ishihara-san thought about thoroughly depicting the story of the first volume so that we could put it into 13 episodes. Generally, when novels get animated, there’s a lot of works that put the content of 2-4 books into 1 cour (12-14 episodes), but with one book, we had to insert elements between scenes to thoroughly depict it. Even if I felt the other way was easier, I would have to stop that in order to meet what Ishihara-san wanted for the composition.

<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/09/eupho0001.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

<strong>– What did you concentrate on while thinking about creating the series composition?</strong>

Well, the peak of the novel was during the re-audition between Reina and Kaori, so how would we set things in motion to arrive at that point? Also, I proposed how we would depict the final part of Kumiko’s plot. The anime would arrive at a temporary final episode through a different path, so I wanted a different arrival and climax for her. Thus, while I was creating the episode structure, I kept in mind that the 12th episode would be Kumiko’s turning point. From the very start, Ishihara-san was fixated on having the final episode’s B-part contain the final performance scene. Since they are part of this work’s very nature and that there was an extraordinarily large emphasis on performances, I was very aware of when I could insert them in the **ning stages of the composition.

<strong>– I was curious: what considerations did you have in mind to change the distance between characters as the story progressed?</strong>

I wanted that sense of moving forward step by step that you get when making a TV anime sometimes. For example, episode 8 holds the summit of Kumiko and Reina’s relationship, so how do I shorten that distance between them as I move to that point? Though the point at the start of episode 2 isn’t in the novel, perhaps I could insert that exchange so viewers will be aware of how far apart they are…. However, I had to stay alert and make allowances here and there so that I don’t overdo it and ruin the novel’s merits. From where we reach the summit for their relationship, I then surged into the novel’s peak of the re-audition and furthermore into Kumiko’s climax point. It’s a bit rough, but you get how that feels.

<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/09/euphobd17.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

<strong>– What do you keep in mind when adding portions that were not in the novel?</strong>

I try to use my imagination as necessary while keeping the contents of the novel in mind. Hazuki is a beginner and she has a wild personality, so perhaps including an episode where she buys the wrong mouthpiece would be appropriate. Sapphire is really self-conscious about her name, so her having to correct Asuka-senpai every time she calls her “Sapphire” would fit. (laughs) As work progresses, my understanding of the characters grow, so I can strongly move them around with my own hand, not worrying so much about the logic. I personally like the president, Haruka, a lot, but unfortunately, she doesn’t have many appearances in the latter half of the novel. (laughs) So when I would write her lines for that part, I used a certain kind of image of her that I had in mind as she speaks. Also the conversation with Asuka and her before the re-audition felt like it came out so spontaneously.

<strong>– Were there any orders from Director Ishihara relating to each episode’s scenario?</strong>

Actually, there weren’t any at all. From the very beginning, he told me ”please write this as freely as you want.” To start I had to figure out what kind of work this was and to put it in a crude state. Using that as a chopping board, we would boil down the contents during discussions with everyone saying “would this character do such a thing?” or “this scene is surprisingly important, isn’t it?”

<strong>– Besides the performance scenes, what elements did you include to make the show seem more like a concert band?</strong>

When I went to observe a concert band, their practicing imagery was something that remained with me. Elements like instruction given to members and how those members responded are portions people don’t see on the stage. That experienced feeling of tension and the sudden rush of sounds pitter-pattering in like a mosaic inside the room is truly unique. Both Ishihara-san and Yamada-san, who I went with to see the band, gave me an order that “[we] want to insert scenes around practicing as much as possible.”

<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/09/euphobd18.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

<strong>– What points in particular did you see while you were observing the band?</strong>

We observed high school and collegiate concert bands and a concert performance. At the start of our observation, the students were performing the “Crescent Moon Dance” piece and we were also able to see them practicing it as well. There were many instances where the instructor would say “play this song like this” and while the students listened to their ex**ation, they would know what to do to make the song sound like what the instructor wanted. (laughs) It’s so much of a positive to see the song being plated and understand how to play that song. I was scribbling notes for what Taki-sensei would say as we were observing them. (laughs) Additionally, the specific phrases the instructor used were memorable. “A bit more stingy” or “More cool.” Someone who’s new to playing instruments wouldn’t know what they’re saying, but it’d be properly communicated to someone who’s played a lot. Also, this is something people may not remember, but try to think back to when you listened to a concert band when you were a student. The tune doesn’t suddenly stop after 2 stanzas, right? At that time, what part is the band practicing? When I listened and heard that in reality, it immediately intrigued me, so I thought it would be great to try and skillfully add that to the scenario. There’s a lot of modern anime shows that have depictions which suddenly float away from you, but this work feels like you thoroughly depict everything about it.

A youthful drama reflecting student hierarchical relationships

<strong>– One of the side aspects of this work was adolescence. What did you have in mind to depict that side of it?</strong>

For us, there doesn’t appear to be any difference between first, second, or third years in high school. But looking back at that time, there was a huge difference that a single year makes. You act like a first year would when you are one and you start to act like a second year when you become one. I remained aware of things like the difference between Reina’s immature conduct and Kaori’s more adult attitude and their subtle differences despite being students in the same decade. At the time I wrote Gotou saying “You’re a first year. Don’t worry about it,” I was thinking I would say the same thing when I was in his position. (laughs) It’s also a bit easy to use club activities as a spot to show the entertaining ups and downs of a scripted drama.

<strong>– Kumiko is a bit disconnected from what you would imagine a protagonist to look like. What issues did you have while you were writing her?</strong>

I’m a similar person to her, so it never felt difficult at all. I’d just write myself as a base and then it would become Kumiko’s lines. (laughs) Can I depict all of the flaws that Kumiko has…. She says just a bit too much, she’s like a cold splash of water on everyone else burning around her, and while she says some profound things, she’s not profound herself. If they aren’t recognized, then Kumiko should be seen as detestable, but it’s not like that at all. Everyone in the staff and cast shared that “Kumiko component” and worked towards the same direction to depict her well.
<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/09/euphobd19.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

<strong>– What impressions remain with you of the depictions of the other characters?</strong>

Perhaps the character who changed the most from the novel is Sapphire. Everyone in the novel (except Kumiko) spoke with the Kansaiben dialect, but Sapphire used it in the most lively and chattery ways. When I changed it to standard Japanese, she became this ordinary character. So then we had to change her tone a bit. After that, as I added Yamada-san’s idea that she “loves rock,” Sapphire became this entertaining character. From the beginning when she says “I’ll risk my life on it,” and nothing else, Sapphire became this necessary character.


<strong>– Now that you’ve seen the completed visuals, what scenes remain impressive for you?</strong>

It’s gotta be the last scene in episode 12 where Taki-sensei confesses to Kumiko “I haven’t forgotten that you said you can do it.” Actually, at the scenario stage, it was “I still truly believe we will go to Nationals,” just like it was in the novel. That was what episode director (Ichirou) Miyoshi-san changed it to in the storyboards and it became this truly impressive line. As a screenwriter, I feel like “I lost!” (laughs)

<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/09/eupho0002.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

<strong>– Please give us your final thoughts after participating in this work.</strong>

This was something truly worth doing. I can say that it’s one of my most notable works. Before this work, I put it as a standard and felt my next work would be indexed according to it. If our fans would continue to forever love this show and watch it again while recommending it, it would greatly please me.









-----

####  结标淡希  
##### 12572#       发表于 2015-9-29 22:07

23号发行的fanbook之前有流出作者炸裂级的对谈内容

####  心之渊  
##### 12573#       发表于 2015-9-29 22:30



[https://ultimatemegax.wordpress.com/2015/09/27/sound-euphonium-roundtable-director-tatsuya-ishihara-series-director-naoko-yamada-author-ayano-takeda/](http://jump.bdimg.com/safecheck/index?url=rN3wPs8te/pG/gmAWiJ6wPuRY8eS695t0Z8Xv/nlZBffB+hZG2dSsWLPAUs00Zcm86RSuWaT+2GVbkgm1kcuW5i4PILzpPfBQmqVFVfGegVlZT6+jYxFiUwPzFkuk4Ii5K2VAHKQDJc28RzENfJv4KRZLWfj/MxXX0zh0D4Job3RyRHW79lAWOOATXnJvdNVF0m7zmg/3KGWoSp+Dg5xp/Wo5ppDuX+/HdJWvVeJDIv4PSaVq54cV8TK2mXBwclKIPmnw7rujmeQ2GiqVKH5PYtbA++P0X75PRSTvptcZbrI9lWblkPrS/VzSI7NL7ug0P/3tRohCXjQqorLBfht+3Y9qHh6BM0y)


这一篇是石原、山田和原作者的

<strong>Sound! Euphonium Roundtable: Director Tatsuya Ishihara, Series Director Naoko Yamada, &amp; Author Ayano Takeda</strong>

This is a translation of the (long) roundtable discussion between Director Ishihara, Series Director Yamada, and Author Takeda that was published in the Sound! Euphonium Official Fanbook (published on September 25, 2015 by Takarajimasha). Thanks to @yuyucow, @tadamari, and @animenewsdotbiz for their comments and reviews.

<strong>Director x Series Director x Author Roundtable</strong>
<strong>Director:</strong>
<strong>Tatsuya Ishihara</strong>

Anime director at Kyoto Animation. Previous works directed include Chuunibyou Demo Koi ga Shitai!, Nichijou, and The Melancholy of Haruhi Suzumiya.
<strong>Series Director:</strong>
<strong>Naoko Yamada</strong>

Anime director/animator at Kyoto Animation. Previous works directed include K-On!, Tamako Market, and the award-winning Tamako Love Story.
<strong>Author:</strong>
<strong>Ayano Takeda</strong>

Author. Debuted with “Today, We Breathed Together” in 2013. Also in 2013, Sound! Euphonium was published; currently there are 3 volumes and a collection of shorts published.


<strong>It’s rare to see an ordinary protagonist among anime characters</strong>

<strong>– Director Ishihara and Yamada-san, what were your thoughts when you first read the novel?</strong>
<strong>Ishihara:</strong> Actually, there had been discussions at a “talking about it” level about wanting to produce a work that was set in Kyoto by people inside our company. With the setting near our company, my true first impression was that I wanted to animate this more and more. (laughs) Also, since I always think about how I would animate something when I read it, I pondered how we would animate the SunFest parade. (laughs) For animation, we would have to animate a lot of people walking and holding instruments. It’d burn a lot of calories watching it.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>My first impression was that the atmosphere felt right somehow. It was depicted lively with lots of adolescent palpitations and breaths, so I was immensely hooked. I thought that it would be good to depict anything where people get fired up and that you could sympathize with the ongoing relationships with the people taking part in it, not just the concert band itself.

<strong>– Takeda-sensei, what were your impressions about your work being made into an anime?</strong>
<strong>Takeda: </strong>At first I had no idea what that meant. (laughs) It didn’t mean that it was a hit, so I wasn’t that startled. Honestly, when I met with the staff for our meeting, we would just talk about various topics.
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>Rather than feeling like it was a business meeting, we had random discussions that made it feel more like an introduction. After that, it was more like steadily creating the setting for the anime for us, but what did it feel like to you, Takeda-sensei?
<strong>Takeda:</strong> It felt like I was talking about my whole family. At first, I was just passing on information about the characters as well as the minor characters, but after a while, I started to steadily pass on settings for the story that I would write. After it was decided to make the novel into an anime, I believe I took some of our talks and put that in the two volumes published afterwards. (laughs)


<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/09/screenshot_2015-09-27-08-41-43.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

<strong>– As you were working on the series, how did you think about how you were going to portray the work?</strong>
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>What do you mean?
<strong>Yamada:</strong> We went a little here and a little there. At the beginning of the scenario stage, there were discussions about putting more gag-type elements in it.
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>Definitely. By comparison, the novel is more a pure story, right? But the broadcast time was one where the people watching were late night anime fans, so I thought about making it have a more manga-type tempo in favor of them. Eventually, we didn’t go that route, but the storyboards for episode 2, which I drew, may have the most manga-type comical gags portrayed. (laughs) When you compare it to the first episode, the tempo definitely feels different. The reason is that the beginning feels more like trial and error still but as the episodes progress, the feeling solidifies into one tempo as well.
<strong>Yamada:</strong> In the novel, Kumiko’s personality is very charming, but she’s a type that isn’t the general anime character. She’s so ordinary feeling; not at all like you’d picture a heroine being. She started to play music because her older sister played it, she worries over the flavor of the ice cream she bought afterwards, and so on. (laughs) If we depicted Kumiko, she’d feel a bit out of place as a character in an anime. But because of that, this was a very fun challenging production.


<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/09/006cropped.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

One page of Ishihara’s storyboards for episode 2


<strong>– She certainly doesn’t feel like she’s the protagonist in an anime.</strong>
<strong>Yamada: </strong>Furthermore, she goes along with the flow, but she’s at the core of the story. One question was how we can bring that out in anime-form.
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>I’d say her outward appearance is also a bit low on the range of late night anime heroines. But when she’s with the other three girls, her height on that range is her tallest point. To comment on what Yamada said earlier, an ordinary protagonist would be a prodigy player or be absolutely awful, but Kumiko plays her euphonium reasonably well. It’s rare to see that type of protagonist for an anime character.
<strong>Takeda: </strong>Actually, there is a real person I modeled Kumiko from. Since she was tall as well, I was pulled by that image of her. Of the other characters, Sapphire also was modeled after someone. The bloody hands incident was an episode that happened entirely in reality.

<strong>– Takeda-san, what was the process for how you put Kumiko as a protagonist character?</strong>
<strong>Takeda: </strong>After I wrote my debut work, “Today, We Breathed Together,” (published in the Takarajimasha Bunko) my editor asked me “what would you like to write about next?” I told them that I wanted to write about an ordinary girl in a concert band and their first response was that it was too ordinary. (laughs) However, I wanted to capture the insides of the people there rather than merely depict the ups-and-downs of club activities. I consciously kept that balance between the two as I wrote and eventually, it felt like Kumiko’s current personality came out. She became the kind of girl you see around who has that strong will of a protagonist and is still able to be recalled in someone’s mind.

<strong>– Was it also a difficult part to portray a too ordinary protagonist in an anime?</strong>
<strong>Ishihara:</strong> It was part of it. For novels, readers have the ability to stick their own kind of love onto the protagonist, but it’s difficult to make anime in that first-person setting. The standard is to get involved in fun things with a protagonist-seeming protagonist in anime. On the other hand, there are group setting styles from the past that have their own charm by depicting each protagonist one-at-a-time like “Two Years’ Vacation.”
<strong>Takeda:</strong> I love that style. When you combine various types of personalities and ways of thinking and not just one, it gradually settles together like a puzzle you can’t quite piece together at first. Each girl has their own traits and when their mutual traits meet, it starts a chemical reaction of entertaining moments. If one girl doesn’t move a certain way, then another girl with a different personality can cover for her. It’s really fun to depict relationships like that. I’m thinking that I’m a reader wanting to constantly watch over them.


<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/07/euphobd12.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

<strong>– After depicting things in the anime, were there any things that you became conscious about?</strong>
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>With it being a 1-cour 13 episode show instead of a film, there’s no practical turning point scene as the episodes go on one-by-one. I thought for a while about various locations to put one in the series. Though we were to divide the novel into 13 episodes from the beginning, I was re-arranging and fine-tuning the contents until the final episode was finished.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>That reminds me, at the first scenario meeting, I clearly remember you and series composer (Jukki) Hanada-san saying “let’s end the first episode with Kumiko kicking Shuichi in the back.”
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>Eventually, that didn’t happen.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>That’s right. I believe you two shook on it, said farewell, and then at the next meeting it was “let’s think about that again.” What happened there? (laughs)
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>The first episode itself has to have a turning point and so ending with Kumiko talking to Shuichi felt a bit lacking in that aspect. Due to that, as we were inserting the flashback scene for the middle school concert, we decided to use that flashback scheme for every episode as well. Incidentally, the original ** in episode 1 was for people to sense that the school song was being played poorly as a link to that concert, but the audience wouldn’t know what the school song for North Uji High was. Thus we thought about how to convey that clumsy playing. Since we wanted to have an entertaining song, we put in the theme from “Abarenbou Shogun.”
<strong>Takeda: </strong>That was an incredibly entertaining moment. (laughs)
<strong>Ishihara:</strong> Modern anime end the first episode with properly raising a question to be answered. The general show would move the story along to the end of our episode 3 where Taki-sensei rebukes the band’s performance by asking “What is this?” However, I thought it fit this show’s tempo to have episode 2 have the students picking their instruments. And there are a lot of works with that kind of tempo who have the protagonist as a beginner. In that instance, Hazuki saved us. With her there, adding a subplot where she previously bought the wrong mouthpiece was a plus to the story. Both I personally, and the likely large number of viewers, with no knowledge of concert band, would purchase the wrong mouthpiece because we had no idea it was wrong. That fundamental mistake would continue to add up bit-by-bit and feel entertaining.
<strong>Takeda: </strong>Sapphire was enjoyable as well with her slightly “old man” elements and her knowledge of music.

Yamada: She’s the type of girl who would cite sayings by musicians, so basically we depicted her as Joe Strummer. (laughs) Thanks to that, we were able to improve the scenario to have her move around more and bring out more of her charm from the novel.

<strong>– Takeda-san, what were your impressions as you read the anime scenario?</strong>
<strong>Takeda:</strong> As I read it, I felt “so you can make an anime like this.” The contents were so enjoyable. I was surprised at Sapphire-chan’s proper Japanese (Note: While all the characters in the novel except Kumiko speak with the Kansaiben dialect, Saphire really uses it.) and her interest in Tuba-kun. (laughs)
<strong>Yamada:</strong> That mascot has the “just right” feeling to put the euphonium in the shadow of a tuba. When I was a child, we would collect “Sylvania Families,” but the series with musical instruments had a tuba included, but not a euphonium. I really remembered it and felt that we could use it as a technique to convey how minor the euphonium is.
<strong>Ishihara:</strong> Did you know what a euphonium is?
<strong>Yamada: </strong>Yes I did. My older sister played one. When she explained instruments to me, she said “It’s a small tuba” and “There’s a lot of tuba merchandise but…..” and her depressed mood is an image that remained with me. (laughs) Eupho-kun has a different facial expression than Tuba-kun; one that matches Kumiko, and is cute too. As I was creating the goods for inside the show, I thought about how to add the character’s charms.
<strong>Takeda: </strong>Horn-chan is also cute.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>There’s also Sax-kun, but Eupho-kun recently came out. (laughs)
<strong>Takeda: </strong>It’d be funny to create a UFO-themed Eupho-kun design. (laughs) Either way, I truly feel thankful these goods were made.


<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/09/euphobd16.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

<strong>Wanting to depict fellowship greater than love</strong>

<strong>– The characters’ distance is a bit different than in the novel. How did you think about that range?</strong>
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>Reina, in the early stages, would touch Kumiko, like point point, during the entire conversation.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>Additionally, we really paid attention to the imagery paying attention to that distance from the beginning when they weren’t close.


<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/09/euphobd14.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

<strong>– It feels like the composition of their distance and the growth of Kumiko is somehow weaved or linked together.</strong>
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>At the beginning, I don’t think it was this deep, but as we were producing the show, perhaps it led towards this direction. They’re different than ordinary friends. It’s like you’re friends with this amazing person and you want to try your best so that you can be on their level. To Kumiko, Reina is that presence.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>The descriptions in the novel when Kumiko sees Reina were so unbearably stimulating. Therefore, I wanted to properly depict that.
<strong>Takeda: </strong>Thank you very much.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>I **ned to measure the amount of force so that I wouldn’t make a mistake, but it felt like the entire detailed atmosphere that I worked so hard to gather between Kumiko and Reina was just released. (laughs) On one hand it was difficult, but it was irresistibly fun to create on the other. I wanted to convey that adolescent uproar of excitation. Kumiko’s the type of girl to be looking around herself constantly and sometimes her depiction of what she sees is interesting. From her point of view, she sees Reina somewhat sensually, but that’s also a characteristic shared by girls too, right?
<strong>Takeda:</strong> (laughs) In almost every work, not just novels, there’s so many that put romance above fellowship, aren’t there? I wasn’t satisfied with that, so I wrote this work thinking of making fellowship above romance. It’s just as Yamada-san says, Reina is a bit sensual from Kumiko’s point of view. It’s something characteristic that a girl would sense and describe. If a man were writing it, wouldn’t it be more like a lusty wolf coming out? (laughs)
<strong>Yamada: </strong>In this world, there’s so much that doesn’t just move because of love for love’s sake.
<strong>Takeda: </strong>Shuichi is special as well, but for Kumiko, Reina is depicted as a presence that is above him. Before Kumiko met her, he may have been her special guy, but now her relationship with Reina is eternal. It’s not just those two; that type of relationship is throughout this entire story. I wanted to show fellowship as this vastly important thing that gets cultivated by mankind depending on each other and working hard in that closed space of club activities.
<strong>Ishihara:</strong> Relating to that description, honestly, Yamada saved us by being present. I don’t know the first thing about girl friendships or fellowships, but I can surmise from this discussion that it’s quite difficult. By all means the way guys look at girls may be depicted in stereotypes. While there is a portion of this work that feels like the processed view guys see, it was important to escape away from that stereotyping.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>There were some points that Ishihara-san felt he couldn’t grasp. Therefore, I worked as the series director so that not only could I provide a feminine intuition for the work, but I could provide another way of thinking for portions that he was able to grasp. Listening to him is also important as well.

<strong>– Were your conversations grounded on Takeda-sensei’s experiences?</strong>
<strong>Takeda:</strong> I previously played in a concert band, so I included that experience. There are a lot of novels about concert band with flashbacks or written from the point of view of an instructor, but how many would want to read a story depicted from the point of view of a real student? Since I was able to write from a new point of someone who hasn’t lost her love of it, I was able to write freely while weaving and mixing in my own experiences. (laughs)


<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/07/euphobd11.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

<strong>– Was that image shared when the anime was being made?</strong>
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>As the setting was in a location near our studios that we know quite well, we talked about wanting to try to make it feel like on-the-spot filming. I was obsessed over the camerawork while making sure that the background and layout of the screen felt like it was from a real camera.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>The locals were surprised. Uji is Uji, but to have North Uji as the setting surprised people that we would go that far to depict it as such. (laughs)
<strong>Takeda:</strong> I had a moment with my editor when I told them about the setting being in North Uji. It was a kind of “maybe we should put in an episode about green tea” moment. (laughs)
<strong>Yamada: </strong>That’s so true. For my screen layout image, I thought it might be better to have the space seem more masculine despite there being girls in the room since there are so many girls in the club. If we did that, we could use stronger colors in the backgrounds.
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>My ideal backgrounds for this production would not feel like they were taken by a digital camera, but processed like how Kodak film used to be. Older film has somewhat narrow latitude (the rate of light exposure), so the contrast is strong and shadowy parts properly sink into the image. As I was saying that to her, Yamada replies “wouldn’t it be better to have the background hues seem more masculine.” Though Yamada and I both love film, the amount of viewers who would support us who love it is unknown, but we went that course anyways. Additionally, there’s a self-documentary atmosphere feeling as well. While it has the quality of a special about concert bands, we very skillfully chased after the appearance so it would have a feeling of a documentary as well. (laughs)


<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/07/euphobd06.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

<strong>– Can you give a concrete way of how a documentary would be shown?</strong>
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>The camera is from a third person point of view. It’s not from one particular character’s point of view; instead it feels like there’s a cameraman chasing after the subjects. There are still some cuts of that left in where I said “I don’t dislike this style” like in the characters being introduced again in the fourth episode.

<strong>– Yamada-san, was there any other proposals that you suggested for this show?</strong>
<strong>Yamada: </strong>For this show, there were a lot of times that we would just say “that’s right” in agreement for something in contrast to disagreeing with each other. Each person has their way of directing, so there were some points of disagreement with the way to use the camera, but the screen layouts we each wanted were similar.
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>I love cameras, so I’m very perceptive when it comes to depth of field or the way to use aperture. We could use soft focus to make the subject stand out more so they would be more beautiful, or we would obscure the background like a gravure photo shot so that the subject would stand out and still be beautiful. I would control for that kind of difference when creating a screen.
<strong>Yamada:</strong> Sometimes that can be used to depict their psychological state besides how beautiful the subject is.


<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/07/euphobd02.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

<strong>– It felt like the scene where the girls are waiting for the walk light to turn green in episode 1 was very impressive photography.</strong>
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>That’s right. It might sound bad to say, but we intentionally blurred the screen. Recently, TV shows and digital cameras are incredibly clear and pretty, but reality is not like that. From our point of view, the background isn’t so clear; it’s a more blurred point of view right? Older film styles let you experience that kind of reality.
<strong>Takeda: </strong>It definitely felt like I was watching a movie. It didn’t feel like so-called modern anime; it felt more like the characters were really living in the real world. Coupled with the performances by the seijyu, the show always penetrates with that beautifully feeling of reality.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>We also used a similar effect in the scene with the sakura tree rows. I asked to film it with a lens similar to how a bad milk bottle would look. Originally, Ishihara-san is the director, but he asked me to draw the storyboards for the first episode, so I was very worried. But when I see Kumiko’s standpoint and think back about it after later events, that sakura tree row scene image comes to mind as a symbol of where she was. I depicted it as Kumiko wondering how long they’ll be remembered while mingling in a guardian’s point of view. Furthermore, I wanted it to be burned into her swirling heart, so I made it feel more like film.
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>It’s generally associated with a simple Photoshop where you gradually remove the detail, but the so-called 2-line boke can be used sometimes when you want something to appear as if you have a bad lens.
<strong>Yamada:</strong> That shaded-off feeling looks magnificent like in the scene where Midori’s waiting at the station in the final episode. I love that representation from the director of photography (Kazuya) Takao-san. He’s able to process images to create a very good creation.


<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/09/002cropped.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

One page of Yamada’s episode 1 storyboards

<strong>– Takeda-sensei, was there any scenes that you wanted to see at the time the anime was determined?</strong>
<strong>Takeda:</strong> I looked forward to seeing the climbing of Mt. Daikichi. Also, while I had a lot of expectations for the show, I watched it with fresh feelings much like an ordinary viewer.

<strong>– The direction for that felt so detailed. For example, the way the water flew was very deliberate.</strong>
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>For an example, if we were to overlap a pretty flower over a girl, it would appear to be more beautiful than the girl, wouldn’t it? We aimed to have a similar effect here.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>Directing is psychological battling. Therefore, one of the points where you show your craft is how much you unintentionally move things around to a point where you affect the feelings of the viewers. For that reason, you study daily and keep lots of things secret. (laughs)
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>Is that so?
<strong>Yamada: </strong>Yes. I think I’ve said a bit too much today, so I’m stopping there. (laughs)

<strong>Presenting musical instruments with a great deal of unknowns</strong>

<strong>– Let’s look back at how you portrayed wind music since it’s one of the themes of this show.</strong>
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>From before we started work on production, we, as novices, underwent various forms of preventions to guard for unforeseen errors in handling or playing of musical instruments. As you’d imagine, we had quite a bit of them. (laughs) Our contrabass stand would inevitably start to lean down on the rightward side when it was on its stand for example. The reason why is because the right side would disengage once we set the sound post onto the pillar supporting it, and so it’d lean down on the right. We had no idea it would do that, did we? (laughs)
<strong>Yamada:</strong> Similarly, when we were told the keynote for our horn was wrong, I immediately went into a panic without immediately understanding what they said. (laughs)
<strong>Ishihara:</strong> We first drew the tuba with its tuning pipe closed too. But during performances, we were able to make alterations to progress somewhat normally.
<strong>Takeda: </strong>I can feel your obsessions from hearing you talk about them. (laughs) Additionally, there’s a lot of re-occurring parts that would surprise you.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>Also, there was a girl who would play the trombone in our studio who said “When I played in concerts, I would close the tuning pipe and intentionally sound different during tuning.” (laughs) After she said that and I replied “hmm, that so,” I quickly went back to correct her work.
<strong>All:</strong> (laughs)
<strong>Yamada:</strong> I was so nervous every time we would bring in experienced musicians for what they would correct. (laughs)
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>But it helped us tremendously to being them to our studio.


<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/07/euphobd03.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

<strong>– Do you have any memories of how you were able to handle the highly energetic performance scenes?</strong>
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>You can’t run away from them.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>That’s right. It may be the charm of this production, but our staff would research how each instrument would perform during those performances. They would try to convey things like the weight of each piston in their drawing.
<strong>Takeda: </strong>That is amazing.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>It’s worth doing that to give this work credit. From the very beginning, Kyoto Animation as a company has pursued finely detailed expressions. Everyone always carries with them that feeling to always do more for a production.
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>It’s tough work, but it helps you clearly present what you’ve sought out. For example, if I were to depict an overhead spaceship, all I would have to go on is my imagination, right? But musical instruments have form and a way to play them that you have to clearly understand.
<strong>Yamada:</strong> It may seem like you do whatever you can to make the image look better, but it also helps make the portions excluding music with universal human relations come together easier too.
<strong>Takeda: </strong>While I was re-reading the novel, I thought about how the beginning performance and the SunFest performance would look. In the story itself, I had to limit the tale to the characters mentioned or else it would get too confusing, but you constructed settings for all the members of the band. (laughs) I was astonished that you would go so far to determine parts and names for everyone.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>That reminds me, when I asked you about the mysterious step for SunFest, you replied that it’s “A certain samba.” (laughs) As I was conveying it to the episode director (Ichirou) Miyoshi-san, it got a bit entertaining.
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>If it was an ordinary production, the animator would want to stop drawing pictures as soon as possible.
<strong>Yamada:</strong> Miyoshi-san is the kind who would resolutely take it on as a challenge. At the time we would decide to give him certain episodes, he’d do a determined pose. At the same time, he might be increasing his resolve not to quit on it. (laughs)


<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/09/euphobd15.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

<strong>– Takeda-san, going through the whole show, what scene is your most memorable?</strong>
<strong>Takeda: </strong>The performance scene with Kumiko and Reina on Mt. Daikichi in episode 8. In the novel, I didn’t insert musical instruments to link the two girls, but I was moved more by the anime scene. Also, the visuals were immensely beautiful.
<strong>Ishihara: </strong>There were a lot of circumstances where we refined the musical performances in the novel. When we had an opinion that an entertaining performance would fit the anime we tried to insert them as much as possible like the performance of the three girls playing “Twinkle Twinkle Little Star” in episode 6 or the duet with Kumiko and Reina in episode 8.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>We included episodes 6 and 8 as episodes from the short story collection. Since the short story collection would be announced during the real-time production of the anime, we actively moved to mix in the episodes during the storyboarding phase. Actually, it felt really good to include the portrayal of Hazuki’s unrequited love in episode 8.
<strong>Takeda:</strong> I’m glad I wrote it. (laughs)
<strong>Yamada: </strong>Ishihara-san and I were glad when Chikao Takigawa showed up.
<strong>Takeda: </strong>I borrowed the names that were attached to them in the anime when writing the story where the guys get together.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>It felt like we were writing an exchange diary as we were working on the anime and then the novels were announced. I would learn that Taki-sensei likes coffee milk and then it’d show up in your writing. (laughs)
<strong>Takeda: </strong>Right. It was very fun.
<strong>Ishihara:</strong> I’ve wanted to ask Takeda-sensei something. The first novel contains elements that affect the second and third novels. Did you include them from the beginning to write a sequel?
<strong>Takeda: </strong>I included them feeling “If I write one, then that’ll be good.” Also, I included meaningful overcoming reluctance scenes because I think stories that resolve things up very clearly are quite nice. Since I was pursuing realism for the first novel, Asuka became this mysterious upperclassman who thinks about various things and that aspect gave weight to her character image. If the novel and anime clearly explained why you don’t know a lot about her, then she wouldn’t be that realistic mysterious upperclassman, would she? (laughs)
<strong>Ishihara:</strong> Along with that way of thinking and what I mentioned earlier about photography, we purposely would use an unclear lens to bring that feeling closer to the viewer. Our thoughts were that it would strengthen that realistic feeling to not bring everything in focus clearly.

<strong>– Please give a message to all the fans about your thoughts that were affected by this work.</strong>
<strong>Ishihara:</strong> I’ve made shows with high school protagonists many times now, but I learned a lot from this work since it was my first time using a concert band as a stage. It’s been a fun production year. I can’t say something profound like it was slowly reliving my high school days all over again but, through the frantic wrestling with this work, I was able to experience something valuable such as that frantic perseverance I felt during that time.
<strong>Yamada: </strong>This work is something similar to taking all the feelings of Takeda-sensei, the staff, and everyone who watched and putting them into one mass eruption. With all that power pushing me forward, I was able to firm my heart and persist in depicting the strong emotions of adolescence. During the various forms of production, it was troubling, but looking back on it, it was quite fun……
<strong>Takeda: </strong>Being able to have a work animated like this feels like I won the lottery. (laughs) Minutely depicting the depths of wind music, bringing each and every character into reality, and furthermore diligently scraping the novel for all information, I’m thankful for everything. Furthermore, I was blessed with the chance to write sequels and safely conclude my work. All of it was a blessing I never knew once it was set to be animated. I truly thank you all.

####  心之渊  
##### 12578#       发表于 2015-9-30 01:40



 本帖最后由 心之渊 于 2015-9-30 21:01 编辑 

吹响！悠风号圆桌会议：监督石原立也，系列演出山田尚子，和作者武田绫乃

官方fanbook（揭载于2015年9月25日）上所载访谈的翻译，感谢@yuyucow，@tadamari和@@animenewsdotbiz 的建议和检查

<strong>动画角色中一个普通的主角是很罕见的</strong>

<strong>-石原桑和山田桑，你们第一次看见这本小说时候的想法是什么？</strong>
<strong>石原</strong>：事实上，曾经有一个仅仅停留在“谈一谈”等级的关于想要由我们公司里的人制作背景在京都的故事的讨论。由于故事设定在我们公司旁边，我第一印象是我越来越想将其动画化。（笑）而且，因为我总是在阅读的时候想着如何将其动画化，所以我一直思考如何动画化SunFes游行的场景，（笑）对动画来说，我们需要描绘大量拿着乐器行进的人。单是看着这个场景就会消耗掉大量的卡路里
<strong>山田</strong>：我的第一印象是不知怎么的气氛非常合适。大量的青春期的悸动和气息描写的非常生动，所以我被深深地吸引了。我认为描写任何可以让人们燃起来东西都是很棒的，你可以在参与其中的人之间不断发展的关系上找到共鸣，而不仅仅是在乐团本身上

<strong>-武田老师，关于你的作品被制作成动画，你有什么感受？</strong>
<strong>武田：</strong>一开始我并不知道那意味着什么。（笑）我不是说那没有冲击性，所以我没有感到震惊。老实说，当我在碰头会和工作人员见面时，我们讨论了各种各样的话题。
<strong>石原：</strong>我们的随机讨论搞得那更像一场介绍会而不是一次商务会议。在那之后，更像是为动画一点点创造设定给我们，不过武田老师的感受是什么呢？
<strong>武田：</strong>那感觉像是我在谈论我的整个家族。最开始的时候，我只是在传达有关主要角色和次要角色的信息，但之后，我开始一点点传达我将要写的故事的设定。在决定将这部小说动画化之后，我坚信我有将我们的谈话的内容加入之后出版的两卷里。（笑）

<img src="https://ultimatemegax.files.wordpress.com/2015/09/screenshot_2015-09-27-08-41-43.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">


先翻了石原山田和武田这篇的开头，明天把它翻完吧
